在電影検查會試映室裏委員甲這段必須剪去委員乙是的但讓我再看一回

小說電影秘密（Ｓｅｃｒｅｔｓ）（九） 197

— 開羅

「要是這樣的話，請你放心好了。我丈夫的意旨，我是絕對不肯阻擋的。」

「這樣很好，謝謝你。」麥汀納茲高興極了。她好似打了大勝仗，欣欣然地走出去。但她還没有出去的時候，約翰已經氣喘喘地跑進來了。他進來先喊了一聲「曼麗」！但是麥汀納茲裝出許多媚態，告訴他曼麗已答應讓他自由。約翰問道「自由讓我自由」？他瞪著眼望著曼麗。

麥汀納茲說：「是的，我愛，你自由了，可以娶我了那不好嗎！」　　「曼麗」！約翰失聲喊道。但是曼麗直立不動，默然無聲地看著他。約翰又回過頭去抓住了麥汀納茲的手臂怒斥道：「你告訴她些什麽？你胡說些什麽？你說出來！

「約翰，不要這樣」！曼麗低聲地勸戒她的丈。約翰聽見了。就立刻將麥汀納茲的手臂放下了望後退了一步。麥汀納茲接著說道？「我告訴她你愛我你情願娶我你要有自由這都是胡說嗎」？麥汀納茲眼中露着一些驕矜的樣子。　　這都是胡說的！這些說，還有許多别的話，都是我說的瞎話」！　　　那女子的態度立刻變了樣子，怒目瞪着約翰道；「好，當了自己妻子的面，就這樣了」！　　「你呌我跪在上帝的面前，我亦是這樣說法。我和你說的都是昏暓時候的胡說。我們從此斷絕關係了，過去了，没有了。」

麥汀納茲聽了，如同背上澆了一盆冷水。她怒氣勃勃地道：「這就是一位正人君子，他還想做一省的省長呢！哼，我到可以將這事表白表白了。你知道不知，我要呌你身敗名裂，並不是難事」她說完了眼中兇光四射逼視著約翰。　　「曉得」曼麗平聲靜氣地道「他深知道。」　　「這段事情登在報紙上，到是一段好新聞。我呌你做不成省長」！麥汀納茲說著，又回過身來，對著曼麗道；「卡頓夫人，你的丈夫你儘管留著他罷，祇要你情願要他」。　　「這樣很好謝謝你」曼麗拿數分以前麥汀納茲的口吻答復她，其中有無窮的意味，在兩個婦人的心中，發生不同的感覺。麥汀納茲退了出去。約翰開了門，羞慚滿面地對著他的愛妻，但是曼麗並不責備他。她說這件事，她早就知道了。她並且知道她的丈夫。雖在數千里外，被女子美色迷惑得神志昏暓的時候，亦未曾一刻忘記過家中的愛妻。這樣一說直使約翰感激她到萬分。（未完）

1933.05.15

Soviet Russia Disregards Good Faith, Sells the Chinese Eastern Railway; Our Foreign Ministry's Full Text of Protest 1

This railway is jointly owned by China and Russia and cannot be disposed of without consent. Please heed the agreement and reconsider your attitude on this matter.

Russian Ambassador Proposes Selling the Railway to Japanese Foreign Minister, Openly Expressing Recognition of the Puppet Organization 2

Japan Firmly Refutes Russian Note 3

Tokyo. Last night, the Russian ambassador met with Foreign Minister Uchida. It is said that the Russian ambassador proposed to Uchida that if the "Manchukuo" authorities decide to purchase the Chinese Eastern Railway, then Soviet Russia could recognize "Manchukuo." (Reuters dispatch, 14th)

Nanjing. According to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, regarding the Soviet Union's proposal to sell the Chinese Eastern Railway, the Foreign Ministry previously, due to uncertainty about the facts, only submitted a note to the Soviet government, urging it to pay attention to China's interests and the provisions of the 1924 Sino-Soviet Agreement. Subsequently, Soviet Foreign Minister Litvinov publicly declared while meeting with reporters that China had lost its rights under the 1924 agreement and frankly admitted that it was preparing to sell the Chinese Eastern Railway. The Soviet government's determination to violate the treaty and harm China's legitimate rights and interests was thus undoubtedly clear. In order to safeguard national rights and the dignity of the treaty, our Foreign Ministry telegraphed Ambassador Yan on the evening of the 13th, instructing him to lodge a serious protest with the Soviet government. It is said that the content of the protest referred to Ambassador Yan's conversation with Soviet Deputy Foreign Commissar Karakhan on the 11th and Soviet Foreign Commissar Litvinov's statement in the newspaper on the same day, stating that the Chinese government was deeply surprised by the opinions expressed by the Soviet authorities. Because these opinions not only show the Soviet government's complete disregard for treaty obligations, but also show the Soviet government's intention to conclude illegal acts with an illegal organization. In the note delivered by Ambassador Yan to the Soviet Foreign Commissar on May 9th, the respective positions of the Chinese and Soviet governments regarding the Chinese Eastern Railway, based on the 1924 agreement, were clearly pointed out. In Article 9, Section 2 of the "Outline Agreement on the Settlement of Outstanding Issues" concluded by the two countries on May 31, 1924, the Soviet government promised that the Chinese government would continue to redeem the Chinese Eastern Railway, and never promised that any other government or force could acquire the railway. Furthermore, the provisions of Section 5 of the same article are very clear, that is, the future of the Chinese Eastern Railway can only be determined by China and Russia, and no third party is allowed to interfere. Therefore, contrary to the opinion held by the Soviet Foreign Commissar, the Soviet Union absolutely has no right to transfer all its rights and interests in the Chinese Eastern Railway to any party it wishes to transfer them to in any way. Furthermore, the Chinese government should ask the Soviet government to pay attention to the promises made by the Chinese and Soviet governments to each other in Article 4, Section 2 of the above-mentioned agreement, that is, neither of the contracting governments shall conclude treaties or agreements that harm the sovereignty and interests of the other contracting government. Recently, the Chinese government has been unable to participate in the management of the Chinese Eastern Railway due to the pressure of superior military force, but China has never and will never give up any treaty or sovereign interests it has in the railway. This change caused by the situation and for which China cannot be held responsible temporarily hinders China from exercising its right to manage the railway, but it does not affect the validity of the terms of the 1924 agreement or the status of the Chinese Eastern Railway. The Chinese government absolutely cannot recognize the Soviet Union's current right to dispose of the Chinese Eastern Railway without China's consent, just as China's consent is needed when the Chinese and Soviet authorities jointly manage the railway. There is no difference. The Chinese government expresses its approval of the Soviet government's desire to maintain peace, but the Chinese government must point out that the current situation in Manchuria is recognized by the whole world as being caused by military aggression. This intimidation is contrary to both the spirit and the letter of the Pact of Paris of August 27, 1928, and the Soviet Union is one of the contracting parties to the Pact. All civilized countries have guaranteed that they will not grant legal or de facto recognition to this puppet organization. Now, without China's consent, and under the current circumstances, abruptly transferring an important means of transportation in Manchuria in the manner proposed by the Soviet authorities is tantamount to the Soviet authorities recognizing an organization declared illegal by the international community and providing assistance to the aggressor. Once this plan is completed, it will be contrary to the Soviet government's declared desire for peace. Based on the above-mentioned legal and political reasons, the Chinese government has to lodge a very serious protest against the Soviet government's proposal to sell the Chinese Eastern Railway and earnestly hopes that the Soviet government will reconsider its attitude towards this issue in accordance with the 1924 agreement. (Central News Agency dispatch, 14th)

Tokyo. After the Soviet Russian government proposed to sell the Chinese Eastern Railway, the Far Eastern political situation of the four countries of China, Japan, Russia, and [Manchuria] will undergo rapid changes. In order to deal with this situation, the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs is taking liaison with the military and all other parties, and is enriching the content of the Asian Bureau to consider all-encompassing strategies. Although the reason for the Russian proposal seems to be to remove the root cause of disputes between Russia and Manchuria, Russia's revolutionary diplomacy has never allowed other countries to be optimistic. Therefore, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs believes that accepting the Russian proposal wholesale is extremely dangerous. Therefore, whether "Manchukuo" or the South Manchuria Railway (Mantetsu) should purchase it has not yet been decided. It will be decided after further observing the attitude of Soviet Russia. It is unclear what the true intention of Russia's proposal to sell the Chinese Eastern Railway is this time. However, it cannot be denied that the Soviet Union's Far Eastern policy is gradually turning to a disadvantageous position. The fact that the Soviet Union is abandoning the Chinese Eastern Railway may indicate that the Soviet Union is retreating from the Maritime Province. From this point of view, the sale of the northern half of Sakhalin in the future may also be realized. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs is determined to implement a policy towards Russia with a proactive and tough attitude, based on the fundamental principle of Far Eastern autonomous diplomacy. (Tokyo dispatch, 14th) Tokyo. Soviet Russian Deputy Foreign Commissar Karakhan handed a memorandum to Ambassador Ota on April 16th to be forwarded to the Japanese government, drawing Japan's attention to the Eastern Railway and wanting to involve Japan in the Eastern Railway issue. The embassy stationed in "Manchukuo" was ordered to investigate the truth. Now that the investigation has been completed, it is clear that the Russian side's statement is completely unfounded. The drafting of a rebuttal response to the memorandum has begun. It is said that the gist of the response is as follows: (1) The Imperial government's policy of protecting Soviet Russian interests in "Manchuria" will not change in the future. However, since "Manchukuo" is already independent, the Japanese government cannot be responsible for the actions of "Manchukuo" officials based on their sovereignty. If it is attributed to the responsibility of Japanese officials in "Manchukuo", it would be a misunderstanding. (2) The dispute over the Eastern Railway is an action taken by "Manchukuo" in accordance with its right to supervise within its own country and has nothing to do with the Empire. Therefore, it is difficult to understand why a protest is being lodged with the Imperial government. (3) However, regarding the Eastern Railway blockade incident and the issue of vehicle ownership, the Imperial government believes that there is no need to respond. However, according to the Imperial government's investigation, Soviet Russia's cutting off the connection between Outer Baikal and the Eastern Railway is an infringement of "Manchukuo's" sovereignty, and the documents published by "Manchukuo" are considered to be correct. (4) It is inappropriate to allege that the fees for the transportation of Imperial troops on the Eastern Railway have not been paid. The reason is that a portion of the fees has already been paid, and the remaining fees have been temporarily postponed due to the fact that the reduction rate for vehicle transportation fees has not yet been decided. (5) The allegations in Karakhan's memorandum are all based on misunderstandings, and the Imperial government has no choice but to dismiss them all at once. However, the Japanese government hopes that the Russian-"Manchukuo" question will be resolved as soon as possible and that friendly relations between Russia, Japan and "Manchukuo" will be maintained and promoted. (Dentsu dispatch, 14th)

Harbin. Today's Harbin Times predicts that the "Manchukuo" Ministry of Communications will restrict the powers of the Chinese Eastern Railway Board of Directors and evenly distribute the management rights of the Chinese Eastern Railway. The Ministry of Communications will also dismiss troublemakers on the railway, revise freight rates, and reorganize the management bureau. As a result, the Ministry of Communications will actually control the management rights of the Chinese Eastern Railway. In the future, the Board of Directors will be composed of five Russian and five "Manchukuo" directors, with a "Manchukuo" person as the chairman and a Russian as the vice chairman. (Reuters dispatch, 14th)

Harbin. The "Manchukuo" authorities and the Russian representative of the Chinese Eastern Railway, Konitzky, met for two and a half hours yesterday afternoon, but the results of the talks have not yet been announced. (Reuters dispatch, 14th)

Harbin. Two Russians recently arrested in Manchuli by the "Manchukuo" authorities have now been brought to this place. One is Apanovich and the other is Malerfanye. According to police circles, a map of the Manchurian military was found on the two men. The two men are currently being investigated by the police authorities and are expected to be charged with military espionage. (Reuters dispatch, 14th)

Harbin. It is said that some Soviet Russians in Suifenhe have retreated into Russian territory, reporting that the Soviet Russians have again received warnings to withdraw from "Manchukuo." Rumors here are that the Soviet Russians will launch a strike on the Chinese Eastern Railway. The police are seriously searching the residences of communists. It is also rumored that the "Manchukuo" authorities have shipped 10,000 pairs of handcuffs to Harbin. This incident has caused panic among the Russian side. Konitzky, the Russian representative of the Chinese Eastern Railway, guarantees that there will be no strike. The police have stopped the search. The situation in Harbin last night was very tense. The police were all fully armed and patrolling the streets, but the night was peaceful. (Reuters dispatch, 14th)

Luan County: Our Army Continues to Retreat; the Enemy is Only Twenty Miles from Fengrun 4

There is a fierce battle northeast of Zhenzi Town

Our Army Destroys the Luan River Railway Bridge to Hinder the Enemy's Advance 5

Peiping. The situation on the front lines has changed today. On the eastern front, the vanguard of our army, in the vicinity of Leizhuang and Guye, He Zhuguo has moved to Xugezhuang to take command, and Wan Fulin has also moved to Lutai. Luanzhou was penetrated by enemy troops on the Pingyu Highway, forming a salient. The troops in that area have been retreating one after another since late last night. The enemy troops advancing along the Pingyu Highway are only twenty miles from Fengrun, and the situation is tense. (Special)

Luanzhou. The superior enemy launched a westward attack across the Luan River. After fierce battles on the 12th and 13th, the Luan River line was breached in the Qian'an area. The enemy is still concentrating all its efforts on attacking westward, with one part detouring to the Pingda Highway and pressing on Fengrun, and another part heading towards Zunhua. This morning, the sound of artillery was intense northwest of Guye Station. There was a fierce battle in the northeast area of Zhenzi Town on the Pingyu Highway. This place is about forty miles from Tangshan. Our army changed to a new position and defended the second line with all its strength, trying to counterattack the enemy against the water. Commander Wan and Commanders He and Wang moved to a certain three places to command. In the Luanxian and Qian'an west of the Lulong River area, our vanguard troops maintained contact with the enemy. This morning, three enemy planes flew thirty miles north of Tangshan to scout the position and dropped several bombs on Chezhou Mountain. (Special dispatch, 14th)

Peiping. Wan Fulin telegraphed on the evening of the 13th, stating that on the morning of the 12th, the enemy crossed the river from places such as Dongzhai, Xizhai, and Jizikou and shelled Shen's army, successively encircling the left wing of our Wang's army. He's division was the first to be threatened, and the division dispatched troops in an attempt to save the situation. Unfortunately, Shen's division completely collapsed, and the flanks were attacked. After several hand-to-hand combats, it was ultimately unsuccessful due to the disparity in weapons. The enemy then approached the left side of Zhang's division, so reinforcements were added to the left wing of Zhang's division, using the night to attack the enemy, in an attempt to save the critical situation. Unexpectedly, the melee lasted all night and failed. One part of our force that advanced towards Liuzhuang by night repeatedly encountered obstacles from the defeated soldiers of Shen's division. This morning, the enemy launched a combined attack on our two units with infantry, artillery, air, and armored vehicles. In the end, due to heavy casualties, it was unable to hold on and has now withdrawn to the rear for reorganization. Subsequently, 囗 division was added, hoping to reverse the battle. Unfortunately, it was attacked by the enemy's armored vehicles and bombed by airplanes. Although it fought fiercely with the enemy for half a day, it was dispersed due to casualties. Weng's division was isolated and engaged in melee warfare with the enemy. At the same time, the enemy facing Wang's army also increased successively. With the danger of the rear being cut off by the enemy moving south, it was decided to withdraw to the right bank of the Zhi River in order to continue the resistance in cooperation with friendly forces. (Special dispatch, 14th)

Luanzhou. From the night of the 13th to the morning of the 14th, military transport vehicles between Tangshan and Luanzhou on the Beipan Road were constantly moving. Passenger cars were delayed. Starting on the 14th, for the sake of driving safety, passenger cars stopped at Tangshan Station. Another train was opened to Guye Station. The Luan River Railway Bridge was damaged to prevent the enemy from using it. Armored vehicles are now guarding Guye Station. The Luanxian government has moved to Tangshan, and the county magistrate and the ten bureau directors have all arrived in Tangshan to work. Our vanguard cavalry in Luan City are responsible for maintaining local order. (Special dispatch, 14th)

Peiping. Six Principles for Implementing the Rural Revitalization Plan 26

Nanjing: The Rural Revitalization Plan was passed by the Executive Yuan's temporary meeting on the 13th. There are six principles for implementation: (1) Affirm that this committee is a design and promotion agency within the Executive Yuan, not an implementing agency. (2) Maintain the integrity of the original administrative system. Departments with original supervising agencies should be handled by the supervising agencies. Departments without supervising agencies should find ways to incorporate them into the existing administrative system. (3) The central and local governments should do their utmost to eliminate all obstacles to rural revitalization. (4) Efforts should be made to complete the coordination of all domestic agencies related to rural areas. (5) The central and local governments should reorganize the original agricultural agencies and funding. As a principle, no new agencies should be added and no additional funding should be increased unless there is a special need. (6) Every effort should be made to utilize existing personnel in the agencies. If insufficient, experts may be specially hired or contracted. (14th Dispatch)

Nepal's New Prime Minister Takes Office, China to Award Medal 27

Sir Austen Chamberlain's Proposal to Blockade Japan Provokes Questioning from Matsuoka 31

Those who say that an economic blockade against Japan can be implemented are no different from inciting a second world war. I wonder how Sir considers this point and would like to hear his opinion. Current Commentary

Declaring an Extremely Urgent Time 36

Is to enter a wartime state, different from peacetime. Since the September 18th Incident, Liaoning and Jilin have been lost, and Heilongjiang Province is on the verge of danger. The nation's territory has been divided, and the people have been ravaged. At that time, we entered a state of extreme emergency. In reason and in urgency, we could not afford to steal a moment of leisure. But the authorities took uncertain measures. The people were not effectively directed. As a result, the disaster spread. The three northeastern provinces were lost, followed by Rehe. Recently, Japanese militarism has actually used our country's extremely moderate resistance as an excuse to launch a large-scale military operation. In addition to the existing five divisions stationed in the northeast, namely the 6th, 7th, 8th, 10th, and 14th Divisions, two cavalry brigades, two mixed brigades, six special garrison units, and other special forces, they have again added two divisions and restored the Lushun naval port. Their challenge is extremely obvious. It does not require divination. When the Japanese army pretended to retreat from eastern Luan, this newspaper wrote an article exposing their conspiracy, pointing out that they would attack Zhangdu and invade Gubeikou. Now, the facts prove that the Japanese army has concentrated its 7th, 8th, and 6th Divisions along the Great Wall, using the 8th Division as the main force to attack and seize Gubeikou, the 7th Division as the main force to attack Xifengkou, and the 6th Division as the main force to invade eastern Luan. From eastern Tianjin to Nantianmen, all have fallen into a state of war. The ancient city of Beiping cannot avoid being threatened by airplanes and feeling the urgency of war. At this time when enemy forces run rampant and the crisis is imminent, even if we try to seek peace and maintain a state of peacetime, can it be achieved? Furthermore, the conflict between the Hui and Han in Xinjiang may come to a temporary end due to Jin Shuren's escape. However, the crisis remains. The rifts have not been eliminated. Even if it comes to an end now, it will certainly not be a long-term solution. Moreover, the powerful neighbors are waiting for an opportunity, and there are still many internal troubles. In addition, Tibet is unsettled, which has been the case for a long time. At this moment, we cannot arbitrarily judge it as "establishing itself."

But the tendency to separate is an undeniable fact. Xinjiang accounts for nearly one-eighth of the total area of ​​the country. Tibet is rich in mineral resources. All of them are the future treasures of our country. Then the current events cannot be ignored. However, looking back at the domestic situation, the rural areas of this country are too ruined. The society is also extremely tired. Few people have hope for the future. Everyone only cares about the present. So-called relief is extremely slow and cannot solve the urgent needs of the moment. More importantly, it cannot stimulate the public's hope for the future. Opening up a new future in the darkness and pointing out the direction. What is even worse is that the youth who will bear the heavy responsibilities of the country in the future are now also going with the flow. A few people cannot correct the momentary mistakes of the majority. They are also intoxicated with dreams, enjoying temporary pleasures, and forgetting the misfortunes of a hundred years. Therefore, the enemy can wantonly invade and act recklessly.

In the future, if the understanding between Britain and the United States is established, international cooperation in capitalism may have considerable use. The competition with Japan will be limited to economic competition. The brutal act of invading China by force will inevitably become more intense. The Soviet Union, in order to pursue its traditional peaceful diplomacy, must maintain its past relations with Japan. In the international arena, our country will become more isolated. Even calls for moral assistance will decline. So what will we do? The only way is to boost our spirits and use all our abilities to regenerate ourselves.

First, from the government to the general public, we should immediately wash away the mistakes of the past and deeply recognize the current disaster. At this time when the enemy army is deeply entrenched and it is impossible to seek good fortune by fluke, we must quickly determine a major plan. (It is impossible to force a peace. What's more, the Japanese warlords are greedy and insatiable. It is impossible to buy short-term peace with daughters, jade, and silk.) Fighting with our backs to the city is the time. Therefore, internally, we should strive to overcome internal contradictions and eliminate disputes that are contrary to the public interest. Take the national struggle as the center and control others. Then, the scattered masses will be easier to gather, and the timid will also stand up when they hear the news. Only then can we suppress the great powers and stop Japan's aggression. Second, whether it is the government or the public, we should first unify our steps and issue an extremely urgent organization. Even if we cannot implement national general mobilization like advanced countries, the upper-level architecture of politics, military affairs, etc., must strive to be agile and powerful. It not only can command its subordinates but also can effectively lead the people in emergency response plans. The production of mobilization must also progress simultaneously with military mobilization, reaching the countryside to plan for national survival with the power of the group, and to control industry and revitalize the countryside. Only then can we fight a mortal battle with the enemy who invades us. Third, although education is slow to take effect, it is the fundamental plan of the country. It should be transformed into emergency education. We must also change the current injection-style education to universal mass education, so that the general adult can immediately transfer to the front line and serve the nation's war. Command the young to become a strong reserve force and bear the heavy responsibility of reviving China. The current war, even if it "fails", if the whole country strives together, the recent future will be able to reverse the decline, compete with the enemy for the final survival, and avenge our humiliation.

German Representative Suddenly Returns to Berlin; General Discussion on Disarmament Postponed 58

The Key to Success or Failure Lies in Germany's Attitude

Germany Persists in Three Major Principles of Disarmament

Hitler Will Make a Statement to the Parliament

Geneva, 13th, Reuters: The German representative to the Disarmament Conference, Nadorni, decided to leave for Berlin tonight to attend the parliamentary meeting. Therefore, Henderson, Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, has decided to postpone the general discussion of the Disarmament Conference from next Monday to next Thursday. It is reported that British Foreign Secretary Simon may come to Geneva to attend the meeting to be held on Thursday. Geneva, 13th, Reuters: The sudden return of German representative Nadorni to the Disarmament Conference in Berlin has delayed the discussion of the Disarmament Conference again. Everyone is quite dissatisfied and indignant. However, all parties are now keeping silent, thinking that it is appropriate to wait quietly for Hitler to make any remarks in the parliament before deciding on a direction. Berlin, 13th, Reuters: The seriousness of Germany's position in world politics is the main topic of discussion among people here. The stock exchange has now felt this impact and has repeatedly encountered setbacks. A semi-official arena here has now published an article aimed at calming people's hearts, saying that German Chancellor Hitler wants to express his opinion on the current difficult problems in German foreign policy in clear words when he addresses the parliament on May 17th. He will not only discuss the latest developments in disarmament, but also discuss the entire disarmament conference. The entire event of the international political situation must be clarified at the time when the World Economic Conference is about to open. Only by eliminating the uncertain weather can the disarmament conference have a sign of success. Germany has three major principles, namely: (1) other countries must substantially reduce armaments, (2) Germany's equal demands must be recognized, and (3) world security must be determined. The article strongly opposes the resolution established in Geneva, that is, the political organizations of German armed forces should be regarded as part of the army, because France has no intention of limiting its weapons or abandoning its heavy artillery units. Berlin, 14th, Reuters: The opinion of German political circles is that the success or failure of the Disarmament Conference depends on the speech delivered by Hitler in the parliament next Tuesday. The extent to which the actions in Geneva can be changed. It is heard that Hitler will protest that other countries have not implemented disarmament and will support the so-called "defense groups." If Hitler's debate cannot move Geneva, then the Disarmament Conference can be said to be "dead."

Not Forgetting National Defense in Disarmament; French Armories Busy Manufacturing Arms Day and Night 59

Paris, 13th, National News: Today, the French Senate

debated the budget bill. When answering questions, Prime Minister Daladier announced that all French armories are currently working under high pressure in order to complete the construction of French eastern defense fortresses as soon as possible. Daladier stated that although France advocates peace and does not reduce armaments, it must also have adequate preparations for national defense to prevent any unexpected events from occurring. The French government is willing to fully supply the army, but will also strive to implement reduction policies to the extent possible. France is a country that loves peace, but its power and just views will never be succumbed to any aspect of oppression. Therefore, a strong military industry and mass production are essential.

Roosevelt Abandons Request to Congress for Authorization to Resolve War Debts 60

World Economic Conference Unaffected; US Maintains Independent Action on Disarmament

Washington, 13th (National Telegram) – US government officials announced to Congress today that President Roosevelt has abandoned his intention to ask Congress for authorization to modify war debts or reach a compromise. Therefore, the US government has directly submitted to Congress for resolution a matter that would have facilitated US progress at the World Economic Conference. Some members of Congress may attend the London Conference. British and American officials generally believe that for the London Conference to be completely successful, an understanding regarding war debts must be reached. However, unless the US Congress itself proposes a solution, it may not be possible to thoroughly discuss it during the Economic Conference. As it stands, the US representatives will likely be unable to propose a solution themselves, and can only quietly listen to proposals from other countries.

The US government's notification to Congress today comes after the US Secretary of State was compelled to inform French Ambassador Lépinay that President Roosevelt felt unable to assume any responsibility for war debts. It is reported that France had proposed to pay the overdue installment from December, but only on the condition that the US declare a moratorium on the installment due in June. The US Secretary of State then informed him that the President had no authority to assume any responsibility, as the President had clearly asked Congress to formally express its opinion on modifying or suspending war debts, but it had not yet done so. The faction in Congress that strongly opposes modification has expressed its views, but the matter has not yet been brought to the floor. The US government knows that if its representatives attending the London Conference do not have the authority to discuss war debts on a broad basis, they will be in a difficult position. However, if President Roosevelt were to ask Congress for the authority to resolve war debts and fail, it would be even more difficult. Therefore, it is better not to ask Congress for authorization.

It is believed that this attitude of the US Congress will not cause the London Conference to fail. US Secretary of State Hull stated today that the main goal of the London Conference is expected to be achieved within two months. Once major issues at the conference are resolved, he believes that exchange rates will stabilize immediately, trade barriers will be reduced significantly, and international relations will improve markedly. However, Hull also hopes that the disarmament deadlock can be resolved before the London Conference opens, as achieving full agreement on economic matters requires first eliminating international suspicions.

At that time, someone asked Hull whether the US would join in sanctions under the Treaty of Versailles if Germany insisted on immediate and complete equality in armaments, leading the Allied powers to invoke the Treaty of Versailles. Hull replied that the US was not a signatory to the Treaty of Versailles, and therefore the US did not need to act according to its provisions. Today, other US government officials commented on the disarmament conference deadlock, saying that the US would not participate in the disputes between the Allied powers and Germany, but firmly opposed Germany's large-scale rearmament. If Germany were allowed to rearm at a time when all countries are focusing on reducing armaments, leading to an increasingly tense international situation, it would not be wise. These two statements show that the US will continue to act independently on disarmament, but its actions may be broadly similar to those of the Allied powers.

Herriot's Account of US Visit 61

Paris, 13th (Reuters) – French representative Édouard Herriot, who had previously remained silent about the results of his visit to the US, made a statement in the financial news today. According to Herriot, US President Roosevelt could deal generously with the war debt issue to the extent of his power. France must repay the debt installment due on December 15 of last year, but this payment can be included in future solutions. The US President will send observers to an international conference, and if this conference can achieve a satisfactory definition of "aggression," then the US President is willing to abandon mutual trade with the aggressor. The US President does not want to express his opinions lightly on treaty revisions, but on the issue of a tariff truce, the US President advocates a truce from April 29 to June 12. However, if the US dollar depreciates, France can adopt exchange surtaxes. He has pointed out to the US President that Germany will soon demand a navy, putting the London and Washington agreement in an awkward situation. He also explained to the US President that the French army and the British navy together form a bulwark for the guarantee of peace and freedom. Herriot had a striking sentence in his article: "I never expected that Germany's demands and Japan's recent declaration would prove my words to be true."

After Formal Declaration of War Between Paraguay and Bolivia, Neighboring Countries Declare Neutrality 65

Bolivia's Arms Supply Cut Off; Will Be Forced to Accept Mediation 66

Asunción, Paraguay, 13th (National Telegram) – The first goal of Paraguay's declaration of war has been fully achieved. Argentina, Peru, and Chile have all formally notified the Paraguayan government that they have declared neutrality. It is expected that Brazil will also declare neutrality within days. It is also heard that these four countries will begin to pressure Bolivia to submit the Chaco border dispute to arbitration. Although the Paraguayan-Bolivian war has been going on for almost a year, in the past two months, the focus of the dispute between the two sides has been on the method of achieving peace. Argentina, Brazil, and Chile had proposed a basis for resolution, and Peru soon joined. However, Bolivia attempted to have a peace plan proposed by the neutral countries committee in Washington, and was even willing to have the case judged by the US Supreme Court. However, Paraguay became indignant upon hearing of the proposal to move the case to a solution outside of South America, and the peace movement failed. Subsequently, Paraguay, because neighboring countries often sold weapons to Bolivia, resolutely declared war. Today, it has achieved its goal. All neighboring countries have guaranteed that they will no longer sell arms to Bolivia. It is expected that Bolivia, now forced to purchase arms completely from overseas, will accept the mediation of Argentina, Brazil, Chile, and Peru, first ceasing hostilities and then beginning peace negotiations. (It is noted that Bolivia is greatly influenced by US capital, while Paraguay has mostly British investment, so the two countries have different diplomatic affinities, and there is the aforementioned dispute over the method of peace.)

Red Fish 68

East London (Reuters) – Fishermen between East London and Durban, Africa, caught three blood-red fish in their nets. They are about a foot long and their color is like the red light of an alarm. They are now stored in the East London Aquatic Animal Institute. The fish's eyes glow and they are very beautiful and rare specimens. Their name is still unknown. The fish are accustomed to living in the high-pressure deep sea, and it is feared that they will not last long in shallow pools.

Page 8

Chief of Staff Yu of Luandong Discusses the Battle Situation; Special Correspondent Geng Ya of This Newspaper 69

Luan County Special Letter. The reporter went to the Qianmen Railway Station on the morning of the 9th, passing through Dongjiaominxiang. The flowers and trees on the roadside were lush and shaded the sun, and the smooth and flat asphalt road was unmatched by the national highway, which was only an inch of land. However, the magnificent palace-style buildings, with their copper-nailed vermilion doors, mostly hung signs of consulates of various countries, and there were blue-eyed, high-nosed guards carrying guns, walking back and forth with composure. As for the so-called "Consulate of the Great Japanese Empire," the Japanese soldiers with red hats, yellow uniforms, and gold trim leaned against the stone lions, held short guns across their chests, and glared at passersby, frequently blowing their short beards under their noses. The Western-style Grand Hotel, which tolerates dirt and filth, is also closely connected to the eye. Zhang Jingyao, the great traitor, was assassinated here the other day by patriotic youths, which shows that traitors, though sheltered in the concessions, will eventually meet on a narrow road and be unable to escape.

Upon arriving at the station, I waited for the joint train from Pingkai to Tangshan at 2:00 PM. Along the way, the wheat seedlings were oily green, the rape flowers were golden yellow, and willow catkins fluttered into the window, dancing like snowflakes. The beauty of nature was truly overwhelming. The half-opened peonies and peonies sold at Fengtai Station could be purchased for two dimes per large bunch of twenty flowers. The fate of the king of flowers, whether precious or cheap, is still in the hands of the flower grower. Thirty or so iron cars were parked at Luobao Station, fully loaded with carts and mules. The villagers who were helping to pull the carts and horses looked at each other across the cars, still smiling foolishly, as if they did not yet know that they would suffer danger in the battle. Passing Douzhangzhuang, most of the farmers who were cultivating the fields were pulling the plough with three people in front with ropes and one person holding the plough in the back. It is not known whether they are unable to raise cattle and horses, or whether the cattle and horses have already served on the front lines. There are countless graves near the stations of Tianjin and Tanggu. Those whose descendants are prosperous have built mounds and hills, occupying a lot of land. If they are not improved, after a few years, the farmland will inevitably be gradually encroached upon by endlessly spreading cemeteries. At the same time, as the population increases, it is doubtful that they will not gradually feel the panic of cultivated land.

When checking tickets on the train, all those who saw military caps and belts were treated equally and were not questioned. Military personnel should purchase half-price tickets according to regulations. Nowadays, when the country is in serious difficulty, there is much to rely on the military, so special preferential treatment is given, which is not without reason. In Tanggu, tall and unparalleled foreign houses are interspersed with flat-headed earthen houses. The number of smoke stacks and Mobil oil storage tanks is also considerable, which shows the development of industry and the deep penetration of foreign capitalist forces. The cries of Yangcun cakes, Tianjin sweet pears, Tanggu prawns, roasted chickens, salted duck eggs, etc., were noisy at each station. However, the passengers seemed to have iron stomachs and were not hungry, and there was no fresh transaction. The train's stopping and starting made countless hawkers come full of hope and leave greatly disappointed. This phenomenon is thought to be due to the fact that the eastbound train only carries a small number of soldiers. If the westbound train is full of refugees, the hawkers' business may not be so deserted.

Dozens of miles out of Tanggu, there is no green grass or few trees. Only the windmills that draw seawater to boil salt are spinning endlessly. At that time, the moon rose in the east sea, and it was reflecting the setting sun in the west mountains. The clear air near the sea made the bright moon appear even more clean. The train arrived in Tangshan and did not go any further. Waiting until 4:00 this morning, I changed to another train. Facing the rising red sun, I sped forward and arrived at Leizhuang, where a lot of flour and straw were piled up. The accompanying stretcher bearers, about twenty or so, got off the train here. It is expected that there must be wounded soldiers here. From here, the stations directly to Luan County are mostly dug with military deep trenches and solid protective works. The train stopped at Luan Station (the train only passes here). Walking five miles west, I entered Luan City. On the way, I saw a military horse stable with a couplet on the door on the right that read, "At the juncture of man and beast, we should strive for self-preservation." The meaning is quite alert. When I visited the headquarters of the 57th Army, Army Commander He Zhuguo happened to be in Ping. Chief of Staff Yu Jianzhang received me and informed me of the battle situation as follows:

"The enemy, under the pretext that our army challenged them, making them tired of running, began a general offensive on the 7th night. The northeast of Luanhe was originally stationed by a certain unit of our cavalry division, which was separated by a river from the enemy army in the east of the river, about seven or eight miles away, and confronted each other. On the 7th night, around 9 or 10 o'clock, the enemy unit used armored vehicles and artillery to cover 400 or 500 infantry and cavalry soldiers, and attacked the left and rear of our army in Beidaihe. At the same time, 20 armored vehicles, more than 200 cavalry soldiers, and more than 100 puppet troops protruded from Damituan Taoyuan to attack our garrison battalion. By the morning of the 8th, the enemy armored vehicles rushed to the garrison battalion station, cutting off the communication between Beijiehe and the garrison battalion. Our cavalry in Beidaihe was difficult to support, and the garrison battalion was lost. It was once recaptured, but was eventually dispersed by the enemy planes dropping bombs violently in the air. Fortunately, our armored car Henan was very active and covered the retreat to the Zhangjiazhuang station area. The enemy is still pursuing. The Japanese and puppet troops in Jielingkou also attacked our Funing on the morning of the 7th. On the 8th, the enemy dispatched more than 400 infantry soldiers from the Pingyu Avenue, and under the fierce cover of artillery fire, they attacked Funing City together. Our garrison, a certain company of the Weng Division, fought hard for the whole day. Except for the company commander and more than 20 people who jumped over the city wall and broke through, the rest were sacrificed. Qian'an, Shuangwangbao, Lulong, and other places were also successively lost under the fierce attack of smoke and cannon fire. Today, the enemy is still attacking the Wenfeng Pagoda south of Lulong City and the Qinglong River area west of the city along the Pingyu Avenue. The left wing of our army and the right wing of the Wang Army have jointly attacked the enemy, and the enemy has succeeded in the above-mentioned places before using five or six armored vehicles and more than 200 cavalry to attack Changli fiercely along the Beining Line this morning. A small number of enemy teams were also found on the North Mountain of the city. Although there was only one day of fighting, the gains and losses have been several times, and both sides have suffered great sacrifices. Our main force has now withdrawn to Shigezhuang and Anshan, and the precautions are very strict. The enemy has flanked the area and concentrated artillery fire on the station. After several hours of fierce fighting, they are now in a stalemate. On the sea surface of the Luanhekou, it was discovered that there were three white enemy ships and five black enemy ships. The actual actions are not yet clear. However, the terrain between Luanhekou and Leting is extremely important, and elite troops have been sent to guard it. In this general offensive by the enemy, the puppet army is responsible for the front railway line, so as to cleverly avoid the responsibility of destroying traffic. The Japanese army relies on sharp weapons and attacks the flanks and rear. The future situation is very dangerous, but the morale is extremely strong, and everyone is willing to fight to the death in every battle."

(Written in Luan City on May 10)

Enemy Attempts to Encircle Luanzhou 70

Japanese troops Advance on Several Routes; War Situation Tense; He Zhuguo Sits in Luanzhou, Stabilizing Military Morale

Special dispatch from Beiping. The Japanese army's ambition for further advances in North China is becoming increasingly apparent from the battle situations in Luandong and Gubeikou in recent days. According to the war reports received today (13th), the situation on the west bank of the Luan River is tense, and battle clouds are densely packed in the Shixia Town area. Since the Japanese army's general offensive, the military situation has become increasingly serious. Japanese planes have flown to Beiping to scout, and people's hearts are inevitably panicked. "The mountain rain is coming, and the wind is filling the building." Rumors are rising like bow shadows in a cup, and the cowardly are rushing to flee to Tianjin, Shanghai, and other places, as if a great disaster is imminent. It is truly pitiful and ridiculous.

The Japanese army drove large numbers of puppet troops to cross the Luan River to attack Leizhuang and Guye. At the same time, the enemy in Lulong and Qian'an also attempted to cross the river, with the intention of encircling Luanzhou and cutting off our retreat. At around 11:00 a.m. yesterday (the 12th), more than 1,500 Japanese and puppet troops and a detachment of field artillery suddenly rushed to the west bank of the Luan River in the direction of Lulong, covering their advance with five bomber planes. They once advanced to the vicinity of Shaheyi, which is only ten miles northwest of the Beining Railway. The sounds of guns and cannons were heard quite clearly in the Leizhuang and Guye areas. Our army's Weng Zhaoyuan's unit rushed to the scene with a regiment, and the two sides engaged in close combat for several hours. By evening, the enemy army, suffering heavy casualties, was unable to support and began to retreat slightly. That night, at Gaotaizi, Japanese troops also crossed the river stealthily, numbering about 3,000, and advanced in several routes. One route attacked Leizhuang and Tuozitou, and fought with our defense forces in Changtianzhuang and Dashiling at night. The situation in Luanzhou was quite tight for a time. Another route of Japanese troops passed through the Pingyu Avenue and clashed with us in Cheyuanzhai, which is about forty miles away from Fengrun. The residents of Fengrun were uneasy, and the atmosphere was tense, and there was some confusion. Most of our troops rushed to the scene, surrounded the enemy, and tried their best to resist. The fierce fighting has not stopped until now. The enemy at Wenfeng Pagoda continued to shell the western side of the river at Shitikai and Tiankai this morning, and the rumbling did not stop until noon. There was no change in the front line.

He Zhuguo is now personally supervising the battle at the front, sitting in Luanzhou. He believes that the enemy forces that are copying to various places west of Luan are not difficult to solve, and military morale is stable. The war on the front of the railway is relatively calm. Our armored vehicles are still patrolling back and forth near Shimen and the Luan River Bridge. After our army changed its defenses at Gubeikou, it engaged in fierce fighting with the enemy in Xiaoxinkailingxia and other places. Our side calmly responded to the enemy, advancing and retreating repeatedly. After fierce fighting all day and night yesterday, the Japanese army attacked us with more than ten tanks again this morning, and the stalemate continued until noon.

The situation in Shixia Town is quite urgent. Japanese planes are bombing everywhere, and countless civilians are killed and injured, which is extremely tragic.

European War Crisis (Roman Correspondence)

Inside Story of the MacDonald-Mussolini Meeting According to British Media 71

France Expresses Displeasure Over British Prime Minister's Visit to Italy

Since Hitler came to power, the political situation in Europe has undergone unusual changes. Nationalism, from brewing to being openly advocated, seems to be pulling the current era back to the 18th century in the course of history. In the foreign policies of various countries, there is almost a tit-for-tat situation, resembling the pre-war situation. Among them, the deteriorating relationship between Germany and France is the most profound manifestation. Moreover, as Japan withdrew from the League of Nations, the authority of justice (due to the inability to sanction atrocities) has diminished, and the control of force has become even stronger. As a result, the clouds of war have spread throughout Europe, and the military crisis between Germany and France is the fuse for the future. Italy's understanding with Germany and Hitler's German spirit would indeed be united in opposing France due to shared interests. However, how many contradictions do Germany and Italy themselves have that are difficult to overcome? Therefore, the situation in Europe is very unstable, and its reflection on the economy is naturally very serious. Unemployed workers have no work, and general consumption power is reduced. (Taking Italy as an example, the number of unemployed people is already over one million.) Tariffs, currencies, etc., are not easy to resolve appropriately. In addition, the financial panic in the United States has also greatly shocked Europe. Therefore, British Prime Minister MacDonald's visit to Rome to meet with the Blackshirt Prime Minister has attracted worldwide attention and is also a major change in European politics.

Looking at past history, Britain, occupying the throne of world finance, indeed has the mentality of "the sun never sets" in its self-esteem and arrogance. However, it could have telegraphed the Blackshirt Prime Minister to ask him to come to London for a meeting. Why did he personally travel to Rome? Little did he know that Britain was shouldering "the banner of world peace, and also for Britain's security. Therefore, Mr. MacDonald rose up, regardless of his graying hair, and dedicated himself to harmonizing the chaos in Europe..." Since the British Prime Minister took the trouble to accommodate, the Italians naturally expressed their welcome. The bold words, "Only the two of us bear the responsibility of maintaining world peace," and "Almost half of the world is unified under Mussoliniism," fully demonstrated the enthusiasm of the Italians and revealed some of their delusions. In reality, the detailed content of the meeting and talks between the two prime ministers is still a closely guarded secret. However, their central issue of discussion must be the revision of the Treaty of Versailles, which is mostly questionable.

Since Hitler formed his cabinet, the movement for Germany to regain its lost territories after the war has gradually become more intense and concrete. Moreover, Italy gained very limited benefits when the Treaty of Versailles was concluded. Therefore, Mussolini, who loves grandeur and success, has long held grievances. Thus, he joined hands with Hitler, who was in distress. Following Germany are countries such as Austria and Hungary. On the other hand, France is the leader, and attached to it are Poland, Czechoslovakia, Yugoslavia, Romania, etc. These two groups are in mutual opposition, breeding the crisis of a second world war. The British Prime Minister, seeing this danger and wanting to seek peaceful means to escape the crisis, knows that the only way to do so is to satisfy the "aggrieved" with some benefits. This is a very clear fact. Indeed, the London Evening Standard published the inside story of the MacDonald-Mussolini meeting. The contents of the amendments they proposed to the "Treaty of Versailles" are roughly as follows: (1) Cut a piece of land in the Polish Corridor, cutting across from the West Polish city of Konik (CBOJNICE) to the East Prussian city of Marienwerder, as the German Corridor and have Germany lay railway tracks.

(2) Romania should cede Transylvania and Banat, previously taken from Hungary, to Hungary.

(3) Yugoslavia should also return the Banat region, formerly occupied by Hungary, between the Danube and Tisza River (TBEISS RIVER), at the confluence of the two rivers, to Hungary.

(4) Yugoslavia should return the old Austrian region of Krainburg to Austria.

(5) The ancient state of Croatia (CROATIA), currently annexed by Yugoslavia, should be allowed to be independent.

(6) The southern coast of Dalmatia (DAIMATIA), such as Herzegovina (HERZEGOVINA) and Montenegro (MONTENEGRO), must be separated from Yugoslavia and merged into Albania (ALBANIA), and placed under Italian protection as a buffer state.

If this proposal is realized, then the German President and Marshal Hindenburg can return to his hometown of East Prussia without suffering the humiliation of crossing the borders of other countries, only through the German corridor. Italy, which has long coveted hegemony in North Africa and control of the Dalmatian coast, can take control from the north. However, what about Yugoslavia? Moreover, in the international balance of power, Italy's power has increased, and France will inevitably be reduced. Since the British Prime Minister first went to Italy, France naturally expressed displeasure. Therefore, France expressed dissatisfaction with the Four-Power Conference, believing that it was the great-powerism of the pre-war era, and that the League of Nations should now be at the center and adopt enlightened international democracy. Even if it is based on great powers, Poland, which is enough to match Italy, should be invited. At the same time, Poland is unwilling to rely on France, so Polish Foreign Minister Beck visited Czech Foreign Minister on April 1, and then went to Prague, Yugoslavia, to secretly discuss with its foreign minister. This is the beginning of the Small Entente's opposition to great powers. Moreover, it is widely rumored that a secret agreement will be established between the Soviet Union and Poland, so the disputes on the European continent are still just beginning. Even if Germany praises Britain as the "savior of the white race," and the British Prime Minister goes to Rome for peaceful purposes, if the above proposal is indeed implemented, I am afraid it will further arouse the struggle of European countries and increase the anxiety of the people. (April 10, Rome)

Panic in People's Hearts in Beiping and Tianjin Enemy Planes Fly Over Beiping Wealthy People Flee One After Another Japanese Aircraft Carrier Discovered at Dagu Port 72

Special Dispatch from Beiping: Enemy planes have been disturbing Beiping for two days, and the citizens feel deeply uneasy. Although the enemy planes did not come on the 13th due to rain, an aircraft carrier was discovered at Dagu Port on the 12th, carrying thirty to forty planes, which is enough to shake the hearts of the people in Beiping and Tianjin. The actual situation of panic in the hearts of the people in Beiping and Tianjin is recorded as follows:

Enemy planes have been disturbing the skies of Beiping for two days, and the general public feels deeply uneasy. Those with wealth and property believe that Beiping can no longer be a comfortable place to live, so they are implementing the plan of "the best of the thirty-six stratagems is to leave." On the afternoon of the 12th, the number of first and second class tickets sold for the special express train to Beiping-Pukou was twice as many as usual, with seventy-nine first class tickets and over one hundred and forty second class tickets sold. In addition, there were even more third class tickets sold. Those who took the express train to Tianjin to seek temporary refuge in the concessions were not included. Starting on the morning of the 13th, the ticket offices at Qianmen Railway Station and travel agencies were crowded with people ordering tickets, vying to be first and fearing to be last, rushing to purchase. The reporter set off again in the afternoon to interview the general situation in the city. Standing at Qianmen Station for about a quarter of an hour, I saw many heavy trucks and rickshaws transporting luggage. On the platform of the East Station, there were already over seventy pieces of luggage (suitcases, bedding, net baskets) with route slips attached, waiting for the train. Only dozens of people stayed in the waiting room. According to the ticket seller, forty-five first class tickets and fifty-nine second class tickets have been sold today. This did not include tickets sold by hotels. On the Pinghan Railway side, there was also a lot of luggage piled up on the platform, mostly for those going to Shijiazhuang. Over fifty first and second class tickets have already been sold. The reporter also went to Dongjiaomin Lane to investigate hotels such as "Hotel des Colonies," "Hotel des Andes," "Hotel Adler," "Grand Hotel des Wagons-Lits," and "Astor House." Not many people have moved in recently, but there are many people storing luggage. According to the accountant of the Grand Hotel des Wagons-Lits, due to the recent Zhang Jingyao case, the concession area has strict restrictions on the admission of Chinese people whose origins are unclear, so Chinese people cannot move in at will. There has been no decrease in the number of visitors to various entertainment venues. Businesses are not accepting valuables, but everything else is as usual. Overall, although the atmosphere in the city is tense, the people's hearts have not reached the level of panic as in the Yuguan Incident.

At 9:00 a.m. on the 12th in Tianjin, an enemy aircraft carrier was suddenly discovered near the lighthouse about sixty miles off the coast of Dagu Port, escorted by three battleships, with several American warships following behind. At about 10:00 a.m., the enemy ship advanced to the sea about thirty miles away from Dagu Port. Our coastal defense authorities observed with binoculars and determined that the enemy aircraft carrier was carrying thirty to forty planes. The ship was named "Notoro" with a displacement of 15,000 tons. At 12:00 noon, the ship sailed back to the lighthouse and docked. At 2:00 p.m., six planes from the ship flew over the vicinity of Dagu Port and reconnoitered for half an hour before returning to the ship. Tonight, the enemy ship used searchlights to peer into Dagu Port. Also, at 2:00 p.m. on the 11th, a gray ship suddenly arrived at Dagu, flying the British flag. Upon inspection by the customs, it was found that the ship was full of Japanese people. The customs inspector immediately asked why they were flying the British flag, but the Japanese did not answer. The customs inspector boarded the ship for inspection and learned that the ship was named "Shin-Kyu." There were no munitions on board. When asked if they were entering the port, they replied that they were, and immediately changed to the Japanese flag. After entering the port, the ship docked at the Dalian Wharf in Tanggu. According to official reconnaissance, the ship was measuring the depth of the sea for the enemy aircraft carrier and checking for reefs to facilitate the enemy ship's sailing. After receiving this news, residents of Tianjin either fled to the British and French concessions or went south en masse. (13th)

Hunan Provincial Capital Establishes City Plan City Area Divided by Fortresses 73

Changsha Correspondence: The population of the Hunan Provincial Capital is estimated to be over 300,000. He Jian has decided to establish a regular city and establish the Changsha Municipal Government. It has been discussed several times in the provincial affairs meetings. Various parties do not oppose the establishment of the city, but due to financial difficulties and the depletion of the people's resources, most advocate that the principle of not increasing the people's burden and not exceeding the original budget of the current Municipal Affairs Office should be followed. Therefore, Cao Bokai, the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, drafted the "Outline of the Hunan Provincial Capital City Establishment Plan" and submitted it to Chairman He of the Provincial Government. He convened one section chief from each of the four departments of civil affairs, finance, construction, and education to hold a joint meeting to discuss and decide on eight city establishment plans, which were announced and implemented immediately. The date for the establishment of the Changsha Municipal Government has been agreed upon as July 1. The city establishment plan is as follows: (1)

The area of Changsha City shall be divided by the boundaries of the fortresses. 1. The east bank starts from Daokou of North Road, the Qingxin Wharf Tie Bridge, and goes east along the west bank of the Liuyang River to Huji Ferry, through Wangjiayuan, Xujiawan, Yangjiashan, Wumeiling, Yalingwang, Jiachong, to Shimapu, then turns west, through Shizui, Dingjiazui, Xinkaipu, Baijiahe, to Houzishi. 2. The west bank starts from Liao Jiayuanzi, goes west, through Guangdong Mountain, Zhangjiaba, to Tuba, then goes north to Zhangjiachong, Caojiatang, Jianfeng Mountain, Xiao Chong Yuanzi, to Heyetang, then turns east again, through Yejipo, out of Zhifang Textile Factory, to Datongling. All around are bounded by fortresses. (2) The Changsha Municipal Government is subordinate to the Provincial Government and is subject to the supervision and direction of the various departments of the Provincial Government according to its duties. (3) The Municipal Government shall have one mayor, who shall be nominated by the Department of Civil Affairs and recommended for appointment upon deliberation and decision by the Provincial Government. (4) The Municipal Government shall establish sections according to its duties, and its organization shall be determined separately. (5) The regular expenses of the Municipal Government shall be specified separately according to its organization, but the maximum amount shall not exceed the current budget of the Municipal Affairs Office. (6) The city shall not establish a separate Public Security Bureau. Matters under the jurisdiction of the Public Security Bureau shall still be managed by the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau. (7) The Changsha County Government shall not be relocated temporarily until the new governance has been selected and equipped. (8) Various donations within the city area, except for police donations that shall still be directly collected by the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, shall be managed and distributed separately by the Municipal Government, and submitted to the Provincial Government for approval and implementation. (May 9)

Xu He Kong Remnant Bandits Roam the Border Between Hunan and Hubei Provinces Repeatedly Suppressed and Heavily Damaged 74

Hankou Correspondence: The border areas of provinces such as Henan, Hubei, Anhui, Jiangxi, Sichuan, and Shaanxi are places where bandits and communists are active. The major forces include Xu Xiangqian, He Long, and Kong Hechong. Xu's bandits recently occupied the border areas of Sichuan and Shaanxi, He's bandits occupied the border areas of Hunan and Hubei, and Kong's bandits occupied the border areas of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi, forming a tripod situation. However, they have been repeatedly suppressed by government troops and suffered heavy damage, with great losses in strength. The recent disturbances of the three groups of bandits and the government troops' preparations for suppression are described as follows:

Xu Xiangqian's Bandits: Xu's bandits previously infiltrated northern Sichuan with elite troops. The Sichuan army, led by Tian Songyao, together with Liu Cunhou, Yang Sen, and other units, made every effort to block and suppress them. The bandits' base areas of Bazhong, Nanjiang, and Tongjiang were successively recovered. The bandits, knowing that they could not penetrate further, retreated to the border between Sichuan and Shaanxi. Those in the border areas of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, originally Xu's old troops, are currently rampant, such as Guangshan, Jingfu, Shangcheng, and Huangchuan in Henan, and Macheng and Huang'an in Hubei, causing widespread disturbances. The burning and killing in Hejia, Wenshu Temple, Xiangdian, Futianhe, and other places were extremely tragic. It is recently rumored that Xu has sent Ji Xun to command via a roundabout route. Xu is also attempting to enter Hubei from the Shaanxi border and join forces with them. As for the bandits' strength, there are the 4th, 9th, and 26th Armies in the border areas of Sichuan and Shaanxi, and the 24th, 25th, and 28th Armies in the border areas of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui. It is recently heard that they have been reorganized. In addition to the Sichuan and Shaanxi armies preparing to attack Xu's main force from both sides, Liu Zhenhua is leading ten divisions to suppress the bandits in the border areas of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, with four divisions responsible for pursuit and six divisions responsible for interception. Liu went to Jiangxi from Hankou on the 11th, personally carrying the bandit suppression plan for the border areas of the three provinces to Chiang for approval and instructions. He will return to his defense post within a few days and order mobilization for suppression.

He Long's Bandits: He's bandits have been entrenched in Shhehe's old nest and the area bordering western Hunan for several months. He claims to be the commander-in-chief and army commander, and is based in Wuyaguan. Duan Dechang and Wang Bingnan serve as puppet division commanders, stationed in various places. Initially, the bandits tried hard to invade Hunan, but after the failure in Yongshun, they did not dare to cross the thunder pool again. Recently, being trapped on the periphery, they thought of finding another way out, so they sent a bandit regiment to infiltrate Honghu. Xu Yuanquan telegraphed and sent the 34th Division Zhang Wanxin's troops to suppress them, and they were quickly defeated. He's bandits were unsuccessful in their plan, but their ambition was not quelled. They sent another unit to continue to invade Honghu, in an attempt to open the route from western Hubei to central Hubei. Zhang's troops are still in the process of suppressing them, and Commander-in-Chief Xu Yuanquan has dispatched boats to facilitate their infiltration. Xu is scheduled to take a plane to Sha within days and then go to the front to supervise the suppression.

Kong Hechong's Bandits: Kong's bandits, originally called the 16th Army, have been disturbing the borders of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi for a long time. Recently, they have been reorganized into the 16th, 17th, and 18th Armies, with Kong serving as the commander-in-chief. They have been rampaging through Tongshan and Xianning in southern Hubei, Xiutong and Lianping in northwestern Jiangxi, and Ping and Liu in eastern Hunan. He Jian, Chairman of Hunan, was first appointed by Chiang as the Bandit Suppression Supervisor of the Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi border, and then as the Commander-in-Chief of the Western Route of the Five Provinces Bandit Suppression, and the bandits were within his suppression range. After taking office, He immediately led his troops to successively occupy the bandit nests of Kong in Yongxian and Li Tianzhu in Ninggang. The general headquarters will be established in Changsha within days and then moved to Yuanzhou, and an order will be issued for general suppression. On the 12th, He telegraphed Hankou to report on the suppression of Kong's bandits and Li's bandits, saying, "Since our troops were ordered to suppress the red bandits in western Jiangxi, they have fled in all directions. The puppet 8th Army and 12th Division under Li Bandit Tianzhu, and more than 20,000 bandits with guns in Lianyong, with five or six thousand guns, were attacked by our Wang Dongyuan Division in Ninggang Yongxian and gathered in Wanlian on Weiyu and other days this month. After a fierce attack by our Chen Guangzhong Division, more than 3,000 people were killed on the spot. They are still stubbornly resisting, and Wang Dongyuan Division has been transferred from Ninggang to Lian to launch a pincer attack. The bandits' spirit has been frustrated. The entire 16th, 17th, and 18th Armies of Kong's bandits were attacked by our Peng Weiren Division in the vicinity of Wan Xiaoyuan last month, and more than 3,000 bandits were killed. After being intercepted by our Tao and Guang divisions, they have now been broken up into smaller units. A unit attempted to flee north to Tongcheng from the border between Ping and Liu, and was repeatedly blocked and heavily damaged by our Li Jue Division and the local troops. They are now being vigorously suppressed. Liuping Yueyang is quiet as usual, and the traffic between Xian and Pu is still safe." (12th)

Recovered Yutian, Killed Many Bandits Remnant Bandits Have Retreated to Jiangxi Border 76

Economic Decline and Industry Depression in Jiangxi Province, Only the Banking Industry is Thriving 77

Nanchang Communication, Jiangxi has been plagued by bandits for years, spreading to eighty-one counties, production has ceased, exports are nonexistent, and the people's livelihood is extremely difficult. In the past, various products such as porcelain, summer cloth, bamboo cloth, paper, tea, and rice had annual export values of several million or even ten million yuan. Since 1927, exports have plummeted. Jiangxi used to be a surplus province, but last year it had a deficit of 600,000 yuan. Stores are deserted, and the countryside is mostly bankrupt. However, amidst this industrial depression, the banking industry alone is thriving. In addition to the branches of China, Central, Shanghai, and Guohuo banks in the province, there are also several banks such as Construction, Yumin, and Municipal. When closing the accounts last year, China and Central each had a surplus of more than 200,000 yuan, Shanghai had more than 100,000 yuan, and even the least profitable Municipal Bank reached 30,000 to 40,000 yuan. The excellence of its business can be imagined. This is indeed an abnormal economic development. The reasons are: (1) Middle-class people from other counties cannot settle down due to banditry, and most of them pack up their belongings and move to the provincial capital, depositing their money in banks at low interest rates. (2) Amidst this wave of rural bankruptcies, there is a tendency for economic power to concentrate in cities. (3) This province used to be a surplus province. Merchants from Shanghai and other foreign ports often used the selling price of various specialties to offset purchases, without having to directly remit cash from the province. Currently, the financial situation is stagnant, and the balance is lost. When purchasing goods in foreign ports, cash must be remitted from the province, and large banks have the opportunity to manipulate this. (4) Because the exchange rate and the ticket price from Shanghai to Hankou have increased, many businesses purchase Shanghai banknotes from Central and China banks to purchase goods. The banknote is higher than cash. At the highest time, each 1,000 yuan banknote required a discount of more than 30 yuan. (5) Small and medium-sized merchants often borrow money from banks due to poor business and tight turnover. The interest rate is higher than the bank's deposit interest rate. Due to these various reasons, the banking industry alone can profit. (May 5th)
