To the Editor: Having read your newspaper on the 12th of this month, the news item titled "French Concession Police Investigation Results of Gao Yatou Murder Case" contains many distortions of the facts, causing Gao Yatou to be unjustly wronged and without assistance. We are submitting a rebuttal news稿 for publication immediately. If it is not convenient to publish it as news, please publish it as a letter to the editor for correction. Sincerely, The Shanghai Barber Industry Committee for Vindication of the Gao Yatou Tragedy, May 14.

The Shanghai Barber Industry Committee for Vindication of the Gao Yatou Tragedy recently saw the news published by various newspapers regarding the announcement by the French Concession Police. They believe that the investigation report and the autopsy process are unsatisfactory. Gao Yatou was only fifteen years old this year and was able to work as a barber. Her physique and energy must be stronger than ordinary people and certainly not that of someone suffering from an illness. The report further stated that "she suffered from lung disease and the cause of death was heart failure, causing her heart to stop beating." A fifteen-year-old child who stands all day with her arms raised to cut hair would cough incessantly if she had lung disease. Not only would customers be disgusted, but she herself would not be able to stand for long. If you do not believe it, ask a strong, healthy person to hold their arms up for an hour and they will be breathless. How much more so for someone who stands all day?

The report also said, "After dissecting and examining the internal organs and external parts of the body, no signs of violence or assault were found." In this case, the committee has sent people to investigate in detail from all sides. (1) Regarding the autopsy, Guo Wanhai, a representative of the deceased's family, personally witnessed two inspections at the scene. First, the abdomen was dissected from the chest to the navel, and the five internal organs were removed, each cut open and examined. Then, the head was sawn open and the brain was sliced and examined. The lower part of the body was not examined. The doctor who performed the examination, even if he could not distinguish whether the injuries were caused by assault or a fall, should have known where the fatal injury was. How could he say that there were no injuries found? The most dangerous parts of the body in a fall are below the abdomen and the scrotum. The hospital and doctors under the authority of the Public Works Department abandoned the examination of the lower part of the body, which is contrary to law and morality. (2) Regarding the cause of death, it was because Gao Yatou forgot to bring her license and ran away in fear. She was chased by a Western policeman in a car, who slapped her twice on the cheeks, causing her to fall. Gao Yatou immediately knelt on the ground to beg for forgiveness. The Western policeman then kicked her with his foot. After being kicked twice, she died on the spot. The crowd saw this uncivilized act and immediately gathered more than a thousand people. The policeman knew that he had caused trouble and fled from Huanlong Road in a car. The crowd followed closely, and the policeman escaped into the Yangtze Motor Company, where he was surrounded by the crowd. There were many people present who were willing to disregard violent oppression and sacrifice their lives to testify and provide detailed accounts of the tragic event. They are all willing to bear the responsibility of witnessing in court in the future. If the report says, "The results of the investigation and autopsy confirm that running was the cause of death. This case is very regrettable, but the police have no responsibility for this matter," according to the above two points, there are considerable facts and responsible witnesses who can prove the facts. Regardless of whether Gao Yatou died instantly under the violent kick of the Western policeman, the recklessness and barbarity of the Western policeman have become ironclad evidence and cannot be denied. If it is said that the French Concession police have no responsibility for this matter, this committee believes that it is a distortion of the facts and expresses its dissatisfaction. In addition to formally requesting a re-examination according to law, we are afraid that readers will be confused by hearsay, so we are making this factual rebuttal. The Shanghai Barber Industry Committee for Vindication of the Gao Yatou Tragedy, May 14.

National Humiliation Week Speech by Mr. Shen Tilan on the May 3rd Massacre (Continued) 131

May 10 at the Youth Conference

Two, The May 3rd Massacre and China's Internal Affairs

Japan's policy towards China has always been to use discord and instigate civil wars to prevent China from unifying. Starting from Yuan Shikai's imperial ambitions, then Zhang Xun's restoration, then Anfu's resurgence, then the Zhili-Anhui and Zhili-Fengtian wars, and then the Guo Songling incident, and the Dagu Fort incident, every internal conflict has involved Japan's conspiracy. The difference is that before the May 3rd incident, Japan only courted one Chinese warlord, but after the May 3rd incident, it courted multiple warlords, forming a situation where Chinese warlords were divided and occupied different regions. This shows the progress of imperialist methods of aggression. After the May 3rd incident, they not only courted multiple Chinese warlords but also were able to court or reject various Chinese warlords at any time and place. Perhaps today they collude with warlord A to defeat warlord B, and tomorrow they collude with warlord B to defeat warlord A. This kind of fickle tactic is more beneficial to them. After the May 3rd incident, Japan paid more attention to the rise and fall of reactionary forces in China. They tried to court these forces, inciting them to expand further, even to spread throughout the country. Therefore, Japan has also replaced the military force of warlords with the bureaucratic politicians and comprador class in China. From then on, they knew to penetrate deep into the masses of China to find opportunities for their aggression. This is a major turning point.

Three, The May 3rd Massacre and Sino-Japanese Diplomacy

Although Yuan Shikai recognized Japan's Twenty-One Demands, the Twenty-One Demands could not be fully implemented after the discussions at the Washington Conference. Starting from the May 3rd incident, Japan believed that in addition to political and economic aggression, military aggression was needed. Coincidentally, the signs of recession had already appeared, and the internal situation in Japan was also conducive to the rise of 武military thought. Therefore, Japanese warlords decided to adopt direct military aggression against China.

The second point is that since the May 3rd incident, Japan's diplomacy towards China has been focused on using "local incidents" to evade responsibility, making the issues unresolved, and gradually taking advantage of the deception to seize rights. This method is used to make the powers speechless, while Japan enjoys the benefits. The Jinan Incident, the September 18th Incident, Jinzhou, Shanhaiguan, Rehe, and even the recent Chahar War since the Jinan Massacre, they have all been resolved using the small "local incident" label!

This is the impact of the May 3rd Massacre on Sino-Japanese diplomacy.

Four, The May 3rd Massacre and the International Community

Before the May 3rd Massacre, Japan's attitude towards invading China was superficially to coordinate with the powers, advocating the open door and equal opportunities. However, after the May 3rd incident, it openly abandoned cooperation and adopted an isolated attitude.

The Northern Expedition of the National Revolutionary Army aroused the fear of the powers, and foreign warships in China opened fire on the Yangtze River in Nanjing. However, Britain had already compromised with China on the surface, and the United States, due to the lack of concrete political power, not only did not prevent the Chinese revolution but also tried to cooperate with the emerging revolutionary forces. During this naval bombardment, the British and American warships fired blanks, while the Japanese warships were loaded with bullets and fired hard! The United Kingdom and the United States have given a principled recognition of China's tariff autonomy, expressing their goodwill; while Japan has been consistently cunning, without a definite expression. Japan's isolated position is very obvious. The advance into Jinan demonstrated the plight of Japanese imperialism and also demonstrated the dominance and arrogance of the self-proclaimed leader of imperialism. They hoped to gain some exchange benefits by means of demonstration when they later saw that the National Revolution was a strong and powerful movement. We know that Japan's two major enemies, one is Britain and the United States, which are competing with themselves and the capitalist imperialist countries especially the United States, and the other is the socialist country of Soviet Russia. Japan's dispatch of troops was to detect whether there were forces of the two major enemies in the Chinese National Revolution that they thought were involved, or whether it was simply a national revolution. This time they confirmed that the Chinese revolution was a national revolution, and they knew that dealing with the United States was their urgent task, not anti-Russian. However, after the September 18th Incident, Japan seemed hesitant to deal with Russia and the United States because the internal contradictions of imperialism have been deepened since the May 3rd incident.

This is the international significance of May 3rd.

After we understand the historical significance of May 3rd, we should get two lessons:

First, Japan hopes that we will not be unified, and we ourselves are not unified. This is because we do not fight for it ourselves. However, the Chinese people are unified. Many of the internal divisions and struggles in China are the fault of the rulers. Therefore, we feel that the regime cannot be revolutionary if it is divorced from the people.

The second is that China's non-resistance to foreign aggression is also the fault of the rulers. Our people have always advocated and practiced resistance. The uprising of the Northeast Volunteer Army after the September 18th Incident and the enthusiastic support of the people during the January 28th Incident all show that the people have a united determination to resist foreign aggression. Therefore, we feel even more that the regime cannot be revolutionary if it is divorced from the people!

The national humiliation we are commemorating now is not the humiliation of the people, but the humiliation of the government! The people themselves should rise up to seek unity and resistance! To shout for the weak and small nations of the world! To fight for the culture of the world! (Recorded by Ye Wenxiong)

Lecture Summary by Dr. Moulins of Germany (Part 2) 134

— Pang Jingzhou

Our Society Should Pay Attention to the Alarming State of Modern Science

Looking back at China, even pots and stoves are lacking during military operations. Even if there are empty gasoline drums, they are probably used as shelters in trenches and may not be used to steam clothes. The third topic on the fourth day was tropical tumors (cancers, carbuncles, etc.). In addition to explanations of various tumors, lantern slides were used to demonstrate patients with various tumors as evidence. Most of them were collected from Africa and India. Therefore, I feel that there are also many cancer patients in China, but they are hidden in remote areas where there is a lack of medicine and no one to study them. In addition, a film was shown about the division of cancer cells, and the proliferation and division of normal cells in various states. This film was taken in a microscope and is called "attack photography." Because the division of cells is actually not as fast as the movement of bacteria, if we were to photograph it at its natural speed, wouldn't we have to shoot a film that lasts for several hours to see his movements clearly? Therefore, this kind of film is taken in sections of the most active state of cell movement and then connected to become a film. On the screen, it only takes ten minutes to see a cell change from one to two to four. When you usually watch movies, you can see the posture of running horses and the shape of movements. You can use photography to make it a very slow movement, then the very slow process can naturally be turned into a very fast movement by this method of splicing. The situation of cell division, in layman's terms, is simply the state of "how a tumor is formed" or "how flesh grows." These facts can all be brought to our eyes by methods, which can be regarded as true evidence and irrefutable academics. In addition, the state of muscle cells trembling when muscles are subjected to current was also shown, which is also very valuable. Incidentally, the situation of ribbons and eye network membrane diseases was also shown.

The fourth lecture on the fifth day was on the misdiagnosis and treatment of amebic dysentery. It proved that this type of dysentery, if not treated thoroughly, will later develop various symptoms, such as constipation, abdominal pain, liver abscess, mental illness, anemia, etc. At that time, the symptoms are far from dysentery, and doctors often fail to identify it. However, the result is that years of chronic disease can be cured by removing the ameba. However, the method of checking feces to determine whether one has ever suffered from amebic dysentery is very careful. Relying solely on the patient's verbal description is unreliable, because many patients have only had one or two episodes of diarrhea, which is not a symptom of dysentery at all, but the root cause is also ameba.

This topic is very important. We know that in Shanghai and the southern provinces, I don't know how many people suffer from dysentery between summer and autumn every year. How can this kind of dysentery be completely cured? Later (often many years later), other branches and sections of symptoms suddenly arise. One must not think that it is still the dysentery虫 at work. On that day, the lantern slides and films showed the pathological anatomy of the intestinal wall of various dysenteries and the active state of amebas. In addition, the state of hookworms entering the human body was also shown. Approximately, hookworms and human skin come into contact and have reached the subcutaneous tissue to the blood within one minute. You can use alcohol to wipe the skin, and part of it has already penetrated. The trial method is to show it with a domestic rabbit.

The topic on the sixth day was about malaria. Unfortunately, I could not finish listening due to a time conflict. Based on the above simple record, I think the readers should have the following feelings. (1) Modern medicine has already been studied to this point, and it is indeed of origin and has evidence. We must not be complacent and say, "My country's four thousand years of medicine is enough to maintain the health of our nation." (2) People's inventions and equipment are all from advocating science. According to our medical education decline and the weak foundation of science, how can we catch up? (3) In particular, the above-mentioned so-called tropical diseases are the most common and prevalent in most of our southern provinces. I don't know how many people should study and suppress them. One more thing to ask you to pay attention to is that the inventors and researchers mentioned by Europeans who come to Shanghai to lecture are many Japanese, but Chinese names are never heard, which is the most painful.

Bedbug Disease 135

— Song Guobin

Current Condition Report

Bedbugs are also known as bed lice because their bodies have a strange odor, hence the name "bedbugs." They are also called "bed lice" because they hide in the gaps in the bed. The body of a bedbug is round and flat, reddish-brown, about two minutes long, and surrounded by many hairs. It lives in dark places during the day and comes out at night to suck human blood. It appears in early summer. The difference between it and ordinary lice lies in the fact that it is hidden during the day and comes out at night, and only appears in summer throughout the year. At the mention of bedbugs, everyone is afraid, and people have generally experienced their power. Everyone expresses an attitude of "deep hatred" towards them and their presence. But what is beyond our expectation is that the more you don't want to be close to it, the more closely it is close to you, which really makes you feel helpless. Bedbugs have an amazing breeding rate. Their kind is distributed among all mankind, specializing in absorbing the fat and ointment of the people, and all at night when people are sleeping, making people lose their sleep. As for people who are a little fat, that is even better fodder for them, which is exactly in line with their psychology of "choosing the fat and devouring."

The sin of bedbugs is not only in sucking human blood and disturbing people's sleep, but it is actually a poisonous insect. It has the ability to inject poison and spread germs. When bedbugs suck human blood, they have two tasks: (1) absorb external food │ human blood, (2) excrete their own poison. When they inject the poison into the human body, the person being sucked immediately develops small red and swollen bumps at the site of the bite, similar to urticaria, especially on the limbs and face, which make you feel pain and itching. Women and people with delicate skin are most likely to have this symptom after being bitten. In the past half month, no fewer than a dozen people have come to see a doctor because their faces are itchy and swollen, thinking it is urticaria. In fact, where is it urticaria? It is actually poisoned by bedbugs.

The above is just the pain and itchiness that bedbugs give us. It is not their biggest sin. Their biggest sin is spreading germs. According to my personal observations over the past eight or nine years, in Shanghai, there is a disease that is popular every year in April and May. This disease is generally a constant fever that continues until it subsides after five to seven days, (starting with chills, subsiding with sweating) after five to seven │ to the eleventh day, there are chills and fever as before, and the fever subsides after another four or five days. This disease is called (returning heat.) If we take the blood of a person suffering from returning heat and examine it, we can see many spirochetes swimming inside. Where did these bacteria come from? Undoubtedly, they were brought by bedbugs. According to previous observations, it was believed that this bacterium was mediated by lice, so it was one of the "poverty diseases." In fact, lice are available in all seasons. In terms of time, the occurrence of this disease coincides with the appearance of bedbugs, and those who suffer from it are not limited to the poor. Sometimes the upper class also suffers from this disease. Lice are only on the bodies of the poor, while bedbugs are available regardless of wealth or poverty, which further proves that bedbugs have the possibility of carrying bacteria. Because the above two diseases are related to bedbugs, I have no way to name them, so I named them: "Bedbug Disease."

Medicinal Virtue 136

— Zhou Luobai

Medical ethics. Doctor Song Guobin of the Song Dynasty repeatedly spoke of it. We can often see his writings on medical ethics in various newspapers. Nowadays, the number of doctors in Shanghai who uphold morality is increasing daily. Actions such as adding consultation hours for the poor and refusing commissions from pharmacies for dispensing medicine are undoubtedly the result of loud appeals. This is indeed a good phenomenon in the medical field. But what about the pharmaceutical field? It is shameful to speak of. Although there are slogans about authentic medicinal materials in Chinese medicine, in reality, not only are most of them not authentic, but some even use Western medicine to make Chinese medicine pills and powders. What is to become of Chinese medicine? Western medicine is even more diverse and full of strange things. Some sell fake goods as genuine products, and some sell inferior goods as superior products. Some sell domestic goods as foreign goods, and some sell foreign goods as domestic goods. Some skimp on ingredients, and others use substitutes. Some even beautifully call it "ancient formula, newly made," using Buddhist teachings to sell their wild man's head. They only recognize profit, and do not consider harming people. This trend has recently become even more downward. Although the government at the time had regulations for managing pharmaceuticals, pharmaceutical merchants once opposed these regulations. However, what they opposed was not the regulations themselves, but aspects of the regulations that did not conform to scientific principles and market conditions. They requested modifications. To this day, it has been shelved for three years. Not only has the management not been implemented, but there has not even been a written response. As a result, generally ambiguous pharmaceutical merchants spare no effort in using inhumane techniques to exploit the nation's interests. Therefore, the lack of cultivating medicinal virtue can be said to be extreme. No wonder foreign pharmaceutical merchants in Shanghai, citing the corruption of the Chinese pharmaceutical industry, have established an "International Pharmaceutical Association." Their stated responsibility is to guide the manufacture of Chinese medicines and improve the development of the Chinese pharmaceutical industry. Alas, what a painful situation! Could it be that before the nation is jointly managed by the international community, the field of pharmacy will be subjected to their control first? Although there are not many pharmacists in our country, there are no fewer than several dozen who practice in Shanghai. Together with the certified pharmacy assistants, there could be more than a hundred people. Why haven't we heard from them? Why not set aside differences, unite as one, join the Chinese Pharmaceutical Association, promote medicinal virtue, seek the construction of pharmacy for the country, and seek the development of pharmacy for society. If there are those who do not uphold morality, whether they are national organizations or private businesses, we can all rise up and attack them. Because the Chinese Pharmaceutical Association is a national academic organization. If it can unite as one, its strength will be greater, and medicinal virtue will be easier to promote. Before there are publicly observed regulations on medicinal virtue, according to my personal opinion, we must first adhere to the four words: "precise," "accurate," "pure," and "clean." These are described in detail as follows. What is meant by "precise"? The products must be precise. It does not mean that only my products are precise, but that I do my best with my knowledge and abilities to produce them. Do not produce crudely and carelessly. For example, when making malt extract or cod liver oil, do not destroy the digestive enzymes in the malt extract, nor the Vitamin A in the cod liver oil. Even more so, do not add MSG and falsely claim it as vitamins. There are many malt extracts and cod liver oils produced in China today, but

Page 14

how many of them retain the digestive enzymes and vitamins without loss? Also, take the sugar coating of tablets as an example. Chinese products mostly follow the method of making sweets, and are easily deliquescent. How many companies manufacture according to pharmaceutical standards, so that they can be stored for a long time without becoming damp? How many pharmaceutical preparations can be manufactured according to the Chinese Pharmacopoeia? These are what should be paid attention to in the word "precise." What is meant by "accurate"? The dosage must be accurate. Do not dilute two pounds of tincture of opium to make three pounds. Do not make one-grain quinine tablets and falsely claim they are two grains. Because if a doctor uses this medicine with a small dosage and it is ultimately ineffective, they will naturally increase the dosage. Or, if they use an accurate dosage, they will use it in the same way as an inaccurate dosage. As a result, the patient's body is overdosed and poisoned. Is this not harmful? Therefore, weighing medicine should be accurate, preparing medicines should follow the pharmacopoeia, and compounding prescriptions should follow the prescriptions. These are what should be paid attention to in the word "accurate." What is meant by "pure"? The raw materials must be pure. It is not only that the cod liver oil sold to the Bureau of Taxation is adulterated with vegetable oil, that the Cuban cigar is mixed with potassium bromide, or that the East sandalwood oil is mixed with West sandalwood oil that can be called impure. All those that do not meet the content specified in the Chinese Pharmacopoeia can be regarded as impure medicines. However,

how many medical clinics in Shanghai today have laboratory facilities? Therefore, I often propose in the New Pharmaceutical Industry Association that the association should set up a laboratory so that shipments can be sent for analysis upon arrival, so that it can be known whether they are pure or not. Recently, there have also been discoveries of foreign merchants selling fake medicines, and this can also prevent deception. These are what should be paid attention to in the word "pure."

What is meant by "clean"? The handling must be clean. It is not only when chicken droppings are mixed in chicken broth or mud is mixed in syrup that it can be called unclean. All hands during manufacturing, containers for storing medicines, and machines for making medicines that have not been properly disinfected can be considered unclean. However, how many clean Chinese pharmaceutical factories are there? And among them, even fewer use scientific methods for manufacturing. Therefore, domestic pharmaceutical products are often criticized for incomplete disinfection. These are what should be paid attention to in the word "clean." Alas, the nation is in distress, and people's livelihoods are urgent. As members of the pharmaceutical community, how can we shirk our responsibility? Why not quickly rise up and promote medicinal virtue to enhance the personality of pharmacists, to increase faith in medicines, to complete the equipment of pharmaceutical factories, and to improve the quality of medicines. In this way, it may not be a way to save the country. It is hoped that the people will have a proper understanding of medicines, and that those people of Korean descent, Japanese nationality, claiming to be American merchants, buying German medicines, these four unidentifiable people cannot run rampant in our Chinese territory. Then the pharmaceutical industry will be fortunate.

Scientific Guide to a Healthy Life 137

— Yu Songjun

(17)

(E) Postpartum Fever

A relatively common and important disease related to reproductive function during the postpartum period is puerperal fever. This disease is caused by infection through wounds in the reproductive organs. During the postpartum period, a woman is like someone with a serious injury, so she is susceptible to infection through wounds. In particular, traditional midwives completely disregard disinfection during childbirth. Even if the delivery is smooth, the uncleanliness of their fingers and tools often predisposes the mother to the risk of puerperal fever during the postpartum period. Severe puerperal fever, even if not fatal, will leave her moaning in bed for months. In short, puerperal fever is a traumatic fever caused entirely by the toxic effects of bacteria parasitic on damaged parts of the reproductive organs. These bacteria contain potent toxins for the human body. When they infect the bloodstream, systemic symptoms occur. If vital organs are affected, death is inevitable. Among traditional midwives, some know that when the perineum is tough and about to obstruct the baby's head, they will use their filthy fingernails to cruelly puncture the perineum and labia. This is the easiest way to transmit infection and is the most frightening thing. There is also a type of midwife who habitually uses iron hooks and other objects full of bacteria to recklessly perform so-called major surgery, often causing the deaths of both mother and child. This is also the result of wound infection. They die before they even develop puerperal fever. Therefore, disinfecting fingers and tools during childbirth is the most important task. How can traditional midwives understand this reason? So they often harm people's lives. The most important method for preventing puerperal fever is to clean the reproductive organs thoroughly. All medical instruments must be strictly disinfected to minimize the spread of viruses. If uterine contraction is weak after childbirth, ergot preparations should be administered to promote uterine contraction and avoid the danger of bleeding. Ice packs can be applied to relieve uterine pain. Large doses of ergot preparations should also be administered at the onset of the disease. In short, prevention methods that are castles in the air cannot be achieved. If you want to fundamentally solve the problem, nothing is better than maintaining the body's resistance, which is to promote excretion and improve nutrition. The method of caring for women suffering from the disease during the postpartum period is also important. First, the patient must be placed in a comfortable position. Second, the body must be kept clean and contamination of clothing and bedding must be prevented. Special attention should be paid to the air and light in the sickroom and the warmth of the patient. Do not be negligent in the slightest.  )Already(Normal Body Temperature

In the normal postpartum process, there is usually no fever. Although the body temperature is slightly higher immediately after delivery, it can return to normal within 24 hours. If the body temperature rises above 38 degrees during the postpartum period, it should be considered a pathological fever. However, an increase in body temperature on the first or second day or the third to fifth day after delivery cannot be generalized. The body temperature during the second week of the postpartum period is two to three tenths higher than usual. The change within a day is also no more than five tenths. Otherwise, it is pathological. What should also be noted is that the body temperature during the postpartum period is very sensitive. Fever is often possible due to extremely minor obstacles or emotional disturbances. Immediately after delivery, the pulse rate increases slightly and the body temperature decreases. The pulse rate also decreases. After three to five days, it drops to sixty beats, or even below forty beats. This reduction is a normal phenomenon. During the first week of the postpartum period, women are prone to sweating during sleep. This is generally due to drinking more fluids, keeping the body warm, or the labor of breastfeeding, and is not unusual. Women often experience chills during or after delivery. This is also within the physiological range. It is generally due to the body's exposure during delivery and the reaction to the loss of heat during the expulsion of the fetus, and should not be regarded as a pathological effect.

Common Knowledge of Diseases Q&A (9) 138

— Cheng Hanzhang

(7) Acute Bronchitis

(Commonly known as severe cold cough)

Q: What is acute bronchitis? A: It is what is commonly called a severe cold cough, or Acute bronchitis in Western medicine. Q: How does this disease start?

A: Because there are usually various bacteria attached to our airways, when the weather is abnormal, suddenly cold and hot, the body's internal resistance to these bacteria decreases, and then a cold occurs, causing acute inflammation of the bronchi. This is the most common cause, but it can also be caused by chemical irritants or dust being inhaled into the airways. Q: Are there any other causes? A: Yes, many infectious diseases such as measles, typhoid fever, influenza, and whooping cough also cause bronchitis. Q: Is there a relationship between bronchitis and age and physique? A: In terms of age, children and the elderly are more likely to get the disease, and physique is also very important. People who are prone to catching colds are prone to bronchitis. Such people feel very terrible in autumn and winter, often for as long as half a year, and some turn into chronic bronchitis. Q: What are the symptoms of acute bronchitis? A: General fatigue, often with headaches, and rhinitis and hoarseness. At first, there is a dry, prickly cough with a tickling sensation in the throat and trachea, like a feeling of injury. Coughing is stronger when inhaling cold air, smoke, or dust, and there is often a slight increase in body temperature and difficulty breathing. Q: Is there any phlegm coughed up? A: A small amount of phlegm is coughed up in the early stages, which is transparent and mucous. From the third day of the illness, the amount increases and becomes opaque, looking very waxy. Q: Does the body have a fever with this disease? A: There is usually no fever, but children often have a moderate increase in body temperature. Q: What changes are there in the lung auscultation? A: When there is a small amount of secretion, dry rales or creaking sounds are heard during inhalation. When there is a large amount of secretion, moist rales are heard. Q: Is the course of acute bronchitis good? A: Most are good, but it also depends on the patient's physique and the health of the lungs. Bronchitis after influenza is often very dangerous. It also feels dangerous for elderly, weak people, those with heart disease, those with kyphosis, or those who already have lung disease.

Q: What is the treatment method? A: First, have the patient rest and make them sweat, give them some hot drinks, take antipyretics or other antipyretics, and add cardiotonics. Keep the room at a suitable temperature and humidity. Apply a moist warm cloth to the patient's chest, or apply heated anti-inflammatory and analgesic ointment. Q: What should be done when there is difficulty breathing? A: Mustard plasters can be applied to the chest. Severe cases can be treated with mustard plastering, which is very effective. It is better for children to use 20 cm of mustard in a cloth bag and put it in the bath water for a warm bath.

Q: What medications should be taken internally? A: If it is not easy to cough up phlegm, expectorants can be taken, such as ipecac infusion, polygala infusion, fennel essence, almond water, ammonium chloride, etc. These drugs should be selected by a doctor in moderation.

Q: What medicine can be used to stop coughing when the cough is severe? A: Cough medicines are nothing more than some medicines that reduce the excitement of the respiratory center. Ordinary people should not take them indiscriminately, and children should pay extra attention.

Q: Is there a bacterial suspension injection to prevent bronchitis? A: Yes, the bacterial suspensions used to prevent bronchitis are now all catarrhal mixed bacterial suspensions (CATARRHALVACCUN. OCOMBINED). It should be injected three or four times, the first injection is 0.2 cubic centimeters, the second is 0.4 cubic

centimeters, the third is 0.8 cubic centimeters, and the fourth is 1.0 cubic centimeters. Q: How long can the preventive injection prevent this disease? A: It can prevent the disease for about four to five months.

Leprosy Common Sense Everyone Should Have Chinese Leprosy Relief Association 139

— Gao Mingqiang

Leprosy is the most cruel disease, and every country in the world has it. Now I will describe the general common sense of this disease as follows. I think it will be enjoyed by readers. 1. Name Leprosy is a chronic infectious disease. The ancient names of our country, such as Feng, Tumor, Great Wind, Heavenly Punishment, and Malignant Disease, are all other names for this disease. It was not until modern times that it was called Great Leprosy or Leprosy. 2. Pathogen The cause of leprosy is the reproduction of a type of microscopic bacterium called bacillus. This bacillus often parasitizes in the skin and nerves of the human body. It was discovered by Dr. Norway Hansen in 1874, so it is named Hansen's bacillus or simply leprosy or bacillus. 3. Symptoms The initial symptoms are red or white spots on the skin, with a darker red border around them. The sensation on the spots is not as sensitive as other parts, or even numb, and there is no sweating. These spots are first discovered on the limbs and gradually spread throughout the body. Another common sign is that the veins on the skin become thicker and feel painful when touched. As the disease worsens, the fingers and toes rot off, the joints become stiff and cannot be bent, the muscles atrophy, the spots ulcerate, the face becomes swollen, and the eyebrows fall off, resembling a sleeping lion, which is disgusting. 4. Transmission Although the route of leprosy transmission is not very clear at present, it is most easily transmitted through long-term and close contact between ordinary people and those with the disease, such as living in the same room, sharing utensils, sleeping together, and eating together with leprosy patients. The common saying that seeing a leper or touching a leper's body can transmit the disease is an exaggeration and is not credible. 5. Treatment There are now symptomatic drugs for treating leprosy, but treatment requires a long period of time to be effective. According to our experience, even the mildest cases require several months or more than half a year of effective treatment before the symptoms can disappear. As for the drugs used, chaulmoogra oil and various preparations of this oil are the first choice. Common methods of use include injection and oral administration. Although the oral procedure is simple, the effect is not as obvious as injection.

6. Prevention Increasing the body's resistance is the fundamental way to prevent leprosy. Special attention should be paid to things such as adequate nutrition, proper exercise, avoiding overwork, and skin cleanliness. If the above-mentioned symptoms are found, a reliable doctor should be consulted for diagnosis. Other precautions include: 1. Avoiding long-term and close contact with patients. 2. Leprosy patients should live in separate rooms and their utensils and clothes should not be mixed with those of ordinary people. If the poor and sick cannot implement the above rules, the only option is to guide them into leprosy hospitals for isolation. 3. Patients must not marry before being proven completely cured by a doctor. 4. The nasal secretions and skin ulcers and pus of patients contain bacilli and should be destroyed. 5. The children of patients must be separated from their parents with the disease immediately after birth. 6. In leprosy-endemic areas, when hiring wet nurses and servants, if there is suspicion, a specialist doctor should be asked to examine whether they have the disease.

Education News Highlights

Ministry of Education Decides to Postpone the National Education Exhibition 140

The Ministry of Education originally planned to hold a National Education Exhibition in the capital during the Double Ten Festival this year. The details have been reported in this newspaper several times. It is now learned that after the new Minister of Education Wang Shijie arrived at the Ministry, he decided to postpone the National Education Exhibition and has ordered the Department of Social Education, which is in charge of this matter, to comply.

Ministry of Education Schedules Qualification Examination for Graduates of Private Middle Schools to be Held in Shanghai, Wuchang, Beiping, and Guangzhou around June 20 141

In order to help graduates of unregistered private middle schools further their education, the Ministry of Education previously held qualification examinations for graduates of unregistered private middle schools. Those who passed the examination were approved by the Ministry of Education to retroactively recognize their graduation qualifications and could take the entrance examinations for colleges and universities. Many people have taken the exam in the past. Last year, it was already decided not to hold the exam again. However, because there are still many graduates of unregistered private middle schools who are at a loss as to what to do, the Ministry of Education has now decided to hold a final qualification examination around June 20 in Shanghai, Guangzhou, Wuchang, and Beiping, and has entrusted the local educational authorities to be responsible for the arrangements.

Ministry of Education Orders Retakes to be Held After the Public Announcement of High School Graduation Exam Results 142

The Ministry of Education issued instructions to the Anhui Education Department, saying, "We have received your submission. In order to avoid having the examinees wait for the results and save on travel expenses, the Department should promptly grade the examination papers after holding the high school graduation exam, and hold re-examinations after announcing the results. The re-examination is a method of assisting students who fail one or two subjects, and should not be postponed until the next exam. Students who still fail one or two subjects in the re-examination should be instructed to take remedial classes in accordance with Article 9 of the Provisional Regulations on High School Graduation Examinations, and should be allowed to participate in the next examination. If the junior high school students still fail the re-examination, they can take the entrance examination as students with equivalent qualifications, but they cannot take the examination with graduation qualifications. High school students must not take the university entrance examination without graduation qualifications. The Department should follow these instructions."

City Education Bureau Regulations on Health Education Exhibition Measures 145

And Measures for Soliciting Picture Exhibits

Instructing All Levels of Schools in the City to Comply

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order yesterday to municipal and registered primary and secondary schools and kindergartens, stating: "This bureau, in order to instill health knowledge and promote hygiene movements, will jointly hold a health education exhibition with the Health Bureau. An order to participate has already been issued. All matters concerning the exhibition date, location, scope of exhibits, and procedures for sending and retrieving exhibits have been separately stipulated. A copy of the measures is urgently issued, ordering compliance." This order.

Health Exhibition Measures Shanghai Health Education Exhibition Measures: 1. The Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau and Education Bureau, in order to instill health knowledge, promote physical and mental strength, promote hygiene movements, and study implementation methods, will hold a municipal health exhibition. All matters related to this exhibition shall be handled in accordance with these measures. 2. The organization of this exhibition is divided into a general affairs department and an exhibits department. The general affairs department is divided into three groups: administration, storage, and publicity, each with a director. The administration group is divided into three sections: public relations, documentation, and general affairs. The storage group is divided into four sections: arrangement, management, registration, and numbering. The publicity group is divided into four sections: editing, solicitation, lecturing, and performance. Each section has a chief executive and several staff members. The exhibits department is divided into three groups: school, society, and reference, each with a director. Each group may be further divided into sections based on the nature of the exhibits. 3. The scope of exhibits for each group of the exhibits department is defined as follows: (1) School Group: A. Kindergarten and Primary School: (1) Central Education, (2) Subject-based Education, (3) Creative Curriculum Teaching Materials, (4) Testing Materials, (5) Self-made Teaching Aids, (6) Life Guidance, (7) Administrative Affairs, etc. B. Secondary School: (1) Administration, (2) Creative Teaching Materials, (3) Self-made Teaching Aids, (4) Teacher and Student Assignments, (5) Creative Sports Equipment and Models, etc. (2) Society Group: A. Anti-Drug: (1) Tobacco, (2) Alcohol. B. Venereal Diseases. C. Infectious Diseases: (1) Leprosy, (2) Gastrointestinal System. D. Family: (1) Mothers, (2) Infants, (3) Preschool Children. (3) Reference Group: A. Books, B. Instruments, C. Models, D. Films, E. Other. (4) Exhibit display is divided into two types: one is for designated or invited participants, whose displays are organized by category; the other is for voluntary participants, whose displays are organized by group. (5)

The exhibition venue will be located at the Puyi Society on Zixia Road, Dadongmen. Office hours are from 8:30 AM to 5:30 PM daily. (6) The exhibition dates are set for June 1st to 3rd, with opening hours from 9:00 AM to 5:00 PM daily. (7) All participants should obtain an exhibit catalog form from the Education Bureau or request it by mail from May 17th. After filling in the details of all exhibits, they should send a representative to the Education Bureau to register between May 21st and 27th, and collect labels to be affixed to the upper left corner of each exhibit. Then, two days before the opening (May 30th) from 2:00 PM, the exhibits should be sent to the venue. (8) Exhibits from all schools and groups should be sent to the venue. (9) When exhibits from all schools and groups are sent to the exhibition for display, the directors of each group, together with the staff of the respective department, will inspect and accept them according to the catalog and registration forms and issue receipts. (10) Once the exhibits have been inspected and accepted, the staff of the exhibiting schools and groups will arrange the displays themselves according to the designated display locations. (11) During the exhibition period, visitors should be received by the respective groups. If there are inquiries, representatives of the exhibitors or reception staff should provide detailed explanations. (12) Exhibitors should bring the original receipt to the exhibition venue within two days after the closing of the exhibition to retrieve their exhibits. The exhibition will not be responsible for storage after the deadline. (13) Exhibits from the Society Group and Reference Group will not be judged. Exhibits from the School Group will be judged. The judging will be based on schools and will be graded as A, B, C, etc. The judging criteria are as follows: (1) Teaching, (2) Moral Education, (3) Psychology, (4) Economics, (5) Accuracy, (6) Eye-catching, (7) Exquisite, (8) Creativity, (9) Practicality, (10) Inspirational, etc. (14) The exhibition will also feature health education lectures, performances, films, and solicit children's creative books, etc., which will be held concurrently during the exhibition period. The measures for these will be determined separately. (15) These measures will be implemented from the date of approval.

Measures for Soliciting Pictures 146

The bureau also issued an order to the principals of municipal and private primary and secondary schools and the directors of kindergartens, stating: "The municipal health education exhibition has been scheduled to be held from June 1st to 3rd at the Puyi Society on Zixia Road, Dadongmen. In order to encourage children in all schools to pay attention to hygiene habits and promote national health, this bureau will solicit student artwork and hygiene pictures from all schools for display at the opening of the exhibition. However, due to the limited space at the display venue, it will be difficult to exhibit all the artwork from the students of each school. Therefore, special measures for soliciting exhibits are hereby established. Each school should select the best submissions and send them to the bureau by May 25th so that preparations can be made for display. In addition to separate orders, a copy of the Shanghai Health Education Exhibition's Measures for Soliciting Hygiene Picture Exhibits is attached. You are hereby ordered to comply with these measures." This order includes the Shanghai Health Education Exhibition's Measures for Soliciting Hygiene Picture Exhibits: 1. The number of student artwork and hygiene pictures selected and submitted by each school is limited to two pieces from each kindergarten, three pieces each from the lower, middle, and upper grades of primary school, and three pieces each from the junior and senior high school stages. 2. The themes of the pictures can be created freely by the students, but should not deviate from the scope of hygiene. 3. The sizes of the pictures are specified as follows: A. Primary School: (1) Kindergarten: 6 inches in length (using the metric system as the standard), 4 inches in width; (2) Lower Grades: 8 inches in length, 6 inches in width; (3) Middle Grades: 10 inches in length, 7 inches in width; (4) Upper Grades: 12 inches in length, 9 inches in width. B. Secondary School: (1) Junior High School: 14 inches in length, 10 inches in width; (2) Senior High School: 16 inches in length, 11 inches in width. 4. All schools must use domestic paper for the selected artwork. The type of Japanese paper is up to them. 5. The selected artwork does not need to be framed. 6. The outstanding artwork selected from each school will be sent by the Education Bureau to the Public Education Hall after the exhibition for display and preservation.

Sun Sijing is Still Well

The Donghua football team, which is about to depart for the Philippines, played a match against the Navy yesterday. Representatives from the HMS Kent also participated. Spring and Autumn

Seeking 166

— Xianxian

"Seeking," in the world, no matter what it is, anything that has to do with the word "seeking" is always a little difficult.

"Seeking a person," even if you write the word "person" upside down, with feet in the air, even if you "prepare funds and wait, and will never break your word," but carrying a foot warmer lid, from the North Market to the South Market, "the person is still nowhere to be found." "Seeking business," "seeking money," "seeking food," is even more difficult. Even if you put on a smiling face, calling "Sir" and "Uncle," "for the sake of my late father," or say it even more pitifully, "save my family," even shedding two lines of tears after the smiling face, still, "I can't help you," "I'll keep it in mind," and that's it. "Seeking a house" is also like this. Your two feet are sore from walking, as if after an 800-mile marathon race, you finally found a house that suits your taste, but "no families allowed," "no children allowed," it's really difficult. "Seeking flowers and asking willows" seems as easy as turning your hand. The streets are full of "flowers" waiting to be "sought." As long as you are willing to raise your hand, why worry about not finding one? However, remembering the "No Urinating" sign at the entrance of the alley, and the "Guaranteed Cure for Gonorrhea and Leukorrhea" advertisement you saw while urinating, you can't help but hesitate in the face of beauty. "Seeking a helpmate," even if you compromise and only require "clean background, decent appearance, basic literacy, regardless of wealth," but after posting a classified ad like a dried tofu for three days, the applicants are either old women or have pockmarked faces, missing teeth, are blind or mute, and you don't dare to accept. "Seeking happiness" is also not easy. Talking and laughing with friends, if it gets stiff, it can lead to quarrels and fights. Seeing someone likable on the street, even if you are old and experienced, if you "use flattering words" improperly, you will surely get a big slap on your face. I seek and seek, but I can never find something easy. One day, I heard a friend say, "The Huangpu River has no lid."

Then I realized, "The easiest thing in the world is to seek death." However, those who try to drown themselves are rescued by the police, and those who take poison are sent to the hospital for treatment. So, "seeking death" is also difficult.

Rural Sketches 167

— Peng

Dressed in a cloak of emerald green, the rural area in May sleeps quietly! Under that warm sunlight, the mulberry trees on the slope have leaves that are as big as palms. A gentle breeze blows through the unripe wheat field, and the wheat ears stir up a wave of green. A farmer carries a basket of grains in one hand and grabs handfuls of grains from the basket, scattering them on the field that has been leveled into several squares. Another farmer is still urging a strong cow, turning the soil in the field with primitive plowing. He occasionally raises his head to look at the neighboring fields: some are sowing seeds, while others have already sprouted several inches of green seedlings. An anxious expression is revealed on his face, and the sound of urging the cow becomes louder and heavier in the quiet space!

A shepherd boy lies on the back of a cow, coming out of the distant tea mountain. He is reminiscing about the "Sangjian Pusang" romances of the past, while singing a mountain song: "Tea-picking girl, flower-picking boy..." The voice is so long and intoxicated, as if trying his best to pull himself back into those sweet memories! "Chicken feathers, rags for sugar!" Shouting, shaking the iron sheet to make a clanging sound. A ragged sugar seller carrying two bamboo baskets passes by the front of the village. Upon hearing this sound, the village women hurriedly run out of their houses, carrying rolls of rags or chicken feathers in their hands. Children follow in groups, drooling and waiting for the sugar to be exchanged. An old, molting dog, curled up in the corner of the house, suddenly rushes out, barking wildly at the ragged stranger with its two bright eyes, "Woof! Woof! Woof!"

A group of ducks are swimming and quacking in a pond! The duck herder, dragging a long bamboo pole, is enjoying the scenery on his own.

Two farmers, having sold their full baskets of cabbage, and exchanged them for some cloth and sundries, are returning from the town, sweating. As they enter the village entrance, they see a woman with disheveled hair standing in front of their house; she is undoubtedly their wife waiting.

A rooster puffs up its wings and stretches its neck to crow: "Cock-a-doodle-doo!" White smoke rises in wisps from the tops of those houses.

A cuckoo calls from the distant dense forest, "Silly Brother! Silly Brother!" Frogs are angry in the field, bulging their round eyes: "Bad! Bad! Bad!"...

The rural area in May sleeps quietly, quietly.

Urban Sketches 168

— Guo Lanxin

In the dim twilight, Tiehua and I stepped into a small wine shop on Gongguan Road. On the street, we saw several shops shouting loudly with big discounts and sales, but there were few customers. Some stood outside the glass windows for a while and then left. Here, you can also see that the city's economy is gradually collapsing, and the prosperity is already showing signs of fatigue, causing the transformation of the era to fall into an inevitable fate. Two young companions who have been struggling hard in the city for several years cannot suppress the sorrow buried in their hearts, and often use bitter wine to numb themselves. They know that drowning sorrows with wine is useless, but we cannot help but use a glass of wine to forget the immeasurable sins, partings, joys, and sorrows of the world for a moment. Outsiders will think it's complaining, but the feelings of those involved are really hard to describe and will not be understood. Slightly drunk, we left the wine shop and walked into Avenue Joffre in the bright streetlights. Avenue Joffre, with its exotic scenery, is filled with joy and laughter, but also with sadness and sorrow. These two different flavors must be carefully experienced by those who walk on Avenue Joffre. At the intersection of Rue Lupan, we saw the New Hawaii Cafe, so we went in with an interest we had never had before. Pushing open the two small doors revealed dim lights, and two Russian waiters greeted us very politely. We went in and chose a seat, ordered two cups of coffee. The small cafe was well decorated. Inside was a music stage. It was still early, and there were not many customers. The music started, and the reddish light, set against the green ceiling, had a special charm. The murals also became colorful. The sad melody filled us with melancholy.

Just as the music stopped, a Russian woman came in. She was old, but still wore rouge and powder, showing off the style of her youth, which made her look ugly. Youth is worth cherishing and being proud of. Perhaps this woman was a noble lady in her youth, beautifully dressed, enjoying luxury, and acting arrogantly, making young men and wealthy young masters adore her. Now everything is over. Everything before is like a decaying dream. Her decaying body and decaying soul are drifting in a foreign land, being trampled on to earn a living. Oh, how pitiful! Finally, after sitting for a while, we left during the music again. The woman was talking to a middle-aged man who seemed to be a date in the shadows of the palm trees. We parted in the night, feeling lost.

Long Novel

Northeast Fourth Company Commander 169

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Six: Sweet and Bitter Love Scene, Cold Observation of Two Sides, Rugged World, Secret Agreement for Three Years

Guizhi still looked at those bowls, seemingly unconcerned, and said: Whether it's a pretense or not, how would I know? But no one is forcing anyone, so what's the point of pretending? For the past six months, you've been saying this and that to me, so I believe you. Is it possible that people don't have daughters to give away? As she spoke, her expression darkened a bit. Jizhi said: Don't be angry, listen to me. Now the world is rugged, and no one knows what will happen tomorrow. I don't know how long I'll be able to do this job, I'm not sure yet, so I'm asking you to wait three years. Guizhi suddenly raised her voice and said: That's it. You know the world is rugged and you're not sure; why are you asking me to wait three years? These few words left Jizhi speechless. He was silent for a long time before lowering his voice and saying: You need to know that my three-year deadline has a meaning. If I can do this job for three years, I can save as much as possible each month, which would be fifty yuan more, six hundred a year, and two thousand in three years. Then I'll have a way. If I can't do it for three years, cut it in half, and I can still save a thousand yuan. At that time, having some capital in hand will make it easier to find a way out and be bolder. With money, everything is easier. If you ask me to agree to a shorter period now, and I can't do it when the time comes, wouldn't that be worse? That's why I'm making the date longer. If I find a way out in a year and a half, then of course we'll get together within a year and a half, so there's no need for three years. Guizhi blushed and said: You misunderstood me. I'm not talking about the timing, I'm worried that something will change over time. First of all, there's my mother. She's not so easy to talk to, she won't let me say whatever I want. When that time comes, if she wants me to do something, can I not do it? Jizhi listened and looked at her with a smile. After a while, he said: What do you mean by "do something"? Guizhi smiled and said: We're talking seriously, why are you joking again? Jizhi said: It's not that I like to joke, it's just that your words are a source of jokes, so I just said a few words. (70)

Urban Wind 170

— Long Sao

Youth cannot be retained, the fragrance of young grape flowers has passed, the May breeze carries the strings of the city, stirring the emotions of young men and women; making them float away in a drunken dream: looking at the sky, tears are rippling in the clouds, silently speechless.

In front of the red light, the sea of people swept away the spring hearts of the masses. In the department store and on the radio, endless sounds of national subjugation are pouring out. People are intoxicated by clothes, candies, cosmetics, perfumes, and silk stockings, unable to open their eyes like a nodding beetle, and thinking about tomorrow. The wind of Venus blows from Sullivan to Marseille, and then floats from the neon lights of the amusement park, over the laughter of the movie theater. The blood-soaked sad songs of vagrants and newsboys on the street corners are floating. The jade skin of modern girls is flaunting. The Ah Q of the times stares with wide eyes, fantasizing about the splendor of cherry blossom women. At the entrance of the pharmacy, full of spring, young wives and unmarried ladies carry a big bag of "her friend" contraceptives, coming out triumphantly. Next to the small Austin stands a anti-Japanese national salvationist, pulling others by the ear and whispering: Contraception saves the country, thank God, may the masses no longer give birth to those reserve slaves of national subjugation! Suddenly, a Japanese military vehicle full of invaders tramples over everyone's heads and drives away. The numb drunkards lower their heads almost to the ground, but soon return to normal, cursing happily! Ah! Victory, victory! The third victory of non-resistance! The urban wind is smiling humorously at the people of May!

Mothers' Knowledge 171

— Peiying

When your children are sick, there is a family, and there cannot be no children. When there are children, it is inevitable that they will get sick. To prevent children from getting sick, the first thing is to make them have a strong body and strong resistance to maintain permanent health. However, children are not fully developed, and it is difficult to obtain strong resistance. Therefore, weakness, insomnia, colds, teething fever, night terrors, etc., are common difficulties for children. However, we know very clearly that paying more attention to children's health can increase the chances of avoiding illness. If mothers can examine their children on a regular basis like doctors, they will definitely get good results. The most obvious effect is that diseases transmitted from companions can be avoided, which are usually not very careful or attentive. Now, because they are discovered through examinations, they can be avoided. In the past, we believed that children would take whatever they saw, and that getting sick was inevitable. Now we know that preventing infection not only requires them to develop a natural resistance, but also to avoid a disease attack in advance. For example, there are good methods such as blood serum or vaccination to defend against scarlet fever, scarlet fever, and smallpox. However, we should not think that infectious diseases are terrible and that other diseases can be ignored, which is not the case. All diseases are terrible and have dangers. As for creating a strong body and strong resistance, rely on the following methods:

(1) The timing of meals should be correctly specified, and the amount of food should be appropriate and average; such as fats, proteins, starches (carbohydrates), liquids, and various vitamins; that is, mineral salts and green pigments such as vegetables, etc., should also be matched, because this food is needed for body growth. (2) Develop a regular habit of excretion, muscle development, energy conservation, and physical fitness. (3) Live in fresh air and sunlight for several hours every day. The clothes worn by children should be kept warm for the hands and feet. (4) Have adequate sleep in a well-ventilated room with good air. (5) Conduct regular health checks, including blood tests, detailed examinations, and confirmation that there is no blood deficiency. Test urine and stool, and explore the abdomen's breath, which is prone to self-poisoning. No matter what kind of illness a child has, the earliest symptoms are almost the same. These symptoms are nothing more than problems with the respiratory system, such as sneezing, nasal discharge, such as nasal mucus, difficulty breathing, and sore throat; or there are more severe symptoms, such as wheezing and coughing in the chest. Fever may also arise from these symptoms. But one thing can be relieved is that from the throat to the ear tube, if it is also involved, causing an irregular high fever, thus restlessness and disturbing sleep, then for the child's ears, there is no need to directly pay attention, because they are young and will not hurt. Gastrointestinal symptoms may also be found at the beginning of any disease, and they are very confusing, because this disease is easy to ignore, and it is not clear for a while what kind of disease it is. There are many phenomena, which are not easy to determine. Some have poor appetite and cannot eat anything, some have vomiting, some have diarrhea, and some have severe constipation. Any kind of phenomenon is enough to cause gastrointestinal disease. There are many mothers who do not understand the principle that children should sleep peacefully when they are sick, thinking that the sick child is already very distressed and should be taught to be happy, playing with toys, crawling on the floor, and even letting him do whatever he wants. They do not know that the reason why children should be made to sleep peacefully when they are attacked by illness is probably for three reasons. First, to preserve his activity and recovery ability, so as to increase the opportunity to restore energy naturally. Second, to prevent the body from catching a cold due to the harmonization of different air in the room, and to avoid the fatigue of the sick child's hyperthermia. Third, avoid fatigue, because fatigue itself is harmful to health. Sleeping peacefully in bed should give up all happy memories and thoughts. At this time, mothers should prepare more things to accompany them, such as beautiful bedding, brightly colored pajamas, exquisite small tables, glass bottles, etc., to induce children's joy and be willing to live quietly in bed. Put a pot of flowers on the shelf, and prepare some good-looking and delicious food, so that children will be happy when they see it, and on the other hand, they will be willing to eat it. The above words are just for reference, not to say that if a child gets sick, it is not necessary to ask a doctor, but to help before asking a doctor, and to preserve the child's vitality so that he can recover faster.
