Free Talk

Self-Reliance and External Force 174

— Yu Dafu

It seems that in Buddhist meditation, there are two types: self-awakening and assisted awakening by external forces. However, what is prevalent in China now is entirely the ideology of relying on external forces. The well-known fact that a certain president seeks gods and worships Buddha, hoping that Bodhisattvas will come to China, need not be mentioned. Even a certain committee member's five-year plan of waiting for Japan to destroy itself is a manifestation of the meditative mind that relies on external forces. Recently, a certain minister brought good news from abroad, saying that if the enemy attacks Peiping and Tientsin, the United States will definitely intervene, so we should lure the enemy deep into our territory! All of these are examples of Chinese people's optimistic thinking based on reliance on external forces. To put it nicely, it is a diplomatic policy of "using barbarians to control barbarians." To put it bluntly, it is a convenient mentality of being lazy, enjoying misfortune, using others as a tool, and governing by doing nothing.

However, while the principles of Heaven are inevitable, human affairs are uncertain. In a Russian novel, there is a coffin maker who, seeing that a seriously ill rich man next door was sure to die, secretly measured his size and made a coffin, waiting to sell it at a high price. However, the rich man's condition improved and he went to a foreign hot spring for treatment, where he eventually died. Isn't our anger at Russia for selling out the Middle East Railway and not coming to fight the Japanese for us the same as the coffin maker's anger? In the past, the declining gentlemen still had the backing of the League of Nations. Therefore, when the enemy slapped my left cheek, I offered my right cheek, saying that we were a gentleman's country that abided by the League's covenants and that etiquette required it. Now, after losing Jehol and surrendering Doolon three times, we have probably reached the point of taking off our pants and asking the enemy to spank us. If we lure the enemy deep again, decide to abandon Peiping and Tientsin, and wait for American aid, it is like the plan of eating arsenic to drug a tiger. Although a gentleman is a gentleman to the extreme, what is the point of a dead gentleman in front of a living villain?

The Person with a Carbuncle on Their Back 175

— Cao Juren

Wang Hongxu's "Complete Treatise on Surgical Diseases": "A carbuncle on the back is a major disease among carbuncles and sores. Those with severe redness, swelling, and pain should be called a carbuncle on the back." When I was young, a small sore suddenly appeared on my back, and I panicked. My father smiled at me and said, "There's no such thing. You're too young." I didn't understand what the relationship was between "carbuncle on the back" and "age." Later, when I read the biography of Xiang Yu, I came to the part that stated "Xiang Yu suspected that Fan Zeng was in league with the Han, and gradually stripped him of his power. Fan Zeng was furious and said, 'The affairs of the world are largely settled, and you can do it yourself. I wish to be granted my bones and return to the ranks.' Xiang Yu agreed. Before he reached Pengcheng, a carbuncle developed on his back and he died." Only then did I suddenly understand.

Fan Zeng was returning east from Rongyang. I wonder what he was thinking about on the road? Perhaps he recalled how obedient Xiang Liang had been when he was alive; even the extraordinary plan to establish the grandson of King Huai of Chu as emperor was something he had devised. Perhaps he recalled when Xiang Yu trusted him, respecting him as "Second Father"; during the Battle of Julu, the lords of the various states honored Xiang Yu as commander-in-chief, how impressive it was. Perhaps he thought of the strategy of having Zhang Han and other surrendered generals guard Guanzhong; it was hateful that those rice sacks, Zhang Han and the others, lost Guanzhong overnight. Perhaps he thought of Xiang Yu's discord with him: he had told Xiang Yu not to let go of the great enemy Liu Bang; but Xiang Yu instead personally led the army to suppress the reactionary forces, exhausting himself, while the great enemy marched straight into Guanzhong, almost endangering the very foundation. Thinking about it, nothing went as planned. At first, "not only does the ruler choose his ministers, but the ministers also choose their ruler," like a fish in water, with endless hope. Now that the magic mirror has been broken, even a long-gowned friend cannot avoid being subjected to the arrogance of those in power. A highly respected old minister, reaching the end of his road, looks like a lost dog in distress. The more he thought, the angrier he became; the angrier he became, the more he thought; he developed a carbuncle on his back and died halfway. Wang Hongxu treated carbuncles on the back, advocating "harmonizing the yang and opening the pores, releasing the cold stagnation," but "harmonizing the yang and opening the pores" is easier said than done. Fan Zeng withdrew too late, was old in years, depressed and uneasy, and his qi and blood were not harmonized. In the end, he was beyond cure, and his fate was pitiful! I sympathize with the person with a carbuncle on their back!

From Fashion Exhibitions to National Products Year 176

— Yang Xingzhi

㈠

The clever entrepreneurs have decided that 1932 will be National Products Year. Therefore, in the newspapers, in the mouths of "celebrities" and "leaders," and in all the large advertisements, we can often see and hear sincere exhortations to "promote national products" and "recover rights and interests." The purpose of these "exhortations" is said to be to "save the country and save the nation."

The customs authorities have also issued warning statistics: last year's import surplus exceeded 550 million taels of silver. Bank business reports all reprinted this figure and issued cries for help. This year, the poor masses are sighing, and the entrepreneurs are also frowning. Everything is infected with the plague of "recession"!

As a result, domestic products have been reduced in price across the board, especially domestic silk and satin. On Nanjing Road, price reduction banners for domestic silk and satin are fluttering in the wind. "The × family is aground × the factory is jointly holding a grand sale, the × family ××× is jointly holding a competitive sale." Foreign loudspeakers and Chinese gongs are desperately shouting from the door towers, and the newspapers are running large advertisements, appealing, exhorting, encouraging, and enticing. Every entrepreneur is trying their best to stimulate the market's purchasing power and entice the people's spending power. It is said that this is for the sake of "the nation"!

㈡

Purchasing power still cannot be stimulated, because poverty has become widespread in society. Therefore, smart people have come up with new tricks, and this is the recent fashion exhibition. Now let me talk about the grand occasion of the fashion exhibition:

The venue is no different from a dance hall: the musicians continue to play music, and electric lights of various colors flash out various colors. The window glass is all dyed emerald green, and the seats are arranged around the perimeter. Wives, young ladies, young mistresses, school flowers, debutantes, and celebrities sit around like screens. Those who cannot sit stand, one layer, two layers, people crowding people, people squeezing people, anxiously waiting, anxiously looking forward. The fragrance of powder and the smell of sweat mingle in the air, and the air becomes a noisy mass. The white-clad waiters from Guanshengyuan are actively moving back and forth in the crowd.

Suddenly, a bright head appears in the crowd, reporting, thanking, apologizing, and saying that Ling Dingding is coming to perform. Ling Dingding is not a dog star.

Ling Dingding appears, a tall man, shouting like an orator: "We must use national products, national products are very good, not using national products is a traitor..." Speaking in a strange voice and gesticulating wildly, the wives and young ladies all laugh, and Ling Dingding also laughs.

Then, the pitiful Qiuxiang, singing a Jiangbei tune in a shrill voice, with beads of sweat the size of beans flowing down her face. Also, learning to dance like a woman, such a big man, twisting and pinching, so the wives and young ladies laugh again, and Ling Dingding also laughs again.

Everyone is still anxiously waiting, the electric lights are flashing their eyes, and the white-clad waiters are coming and going even more vigorously. The wives and young ladies are a little impatient.

Finally, the stars performing the fashion show come, squeezing from the crowd to the center of the venue, one, two, five, eight, stars, queens, national fashion, circling the venue once, so everyone shouts madly, those sitting in the middle squeeze forward, those standing stand on chairs, necks stretched, eyes widened, people squeezing people, people pressing people, hundreds of eyes are fixed on the eight in the center of the venue, eight pieces of fashion, eight advertisements, the photographer is also busy adjusting the light, busy installing the lens, the eight are lined up in a row, the venue is a noisy mass, only a few wooden clothing racks stand upright in the corner of the venue, strangely deserted. Someone whispers in my ear, "Good heavens, a living advertisement, a living clothes rack"!

"The advertisement" goes in, it's over, everyone is refreshed and relieved, takes a long breath, turns around and squeezes, squeezes out of the door.

㈢

Living advertisements are not only a kind of enticement, a kind of encouragement, they are simply a kind of pressure, forcing people to buy, buy, buy. Waste, as Lhetragedyolwaste describes in his life, is an excerpt from East Hillot's account. He said that some advertisements advised him to eat more bread, some advised him to eat more raisins, some advised him to take the train more often, and some advised him to stay at home more often... only no one advised him to use more coffins!

Who can accept all the advice? What a ridiculous trick!

Waste, everything is wasted without hesitation. This world is indeed overfed; but most people are crying out in hunger and cold. Even living advertisements cannot stimulate their minimum purchasing power. Capitalists and the poor masses are frowning. How desolate this world is!

Random Words from Juju 177

— Zizhan

(Twenty-seven) A Glimpse of the Dance Hall

Singing and dancing constantly, they speak of the Southern Dynasties,

Emerald feathers bright...

Unparalleled scholars...

This old man only sings "Nian Nu Jiao."

One evening, I and my friend returned from a glimpse of the dance hall, and thus recalled Mr. Xiong Xiling's words in "Nian Nu Jiao," and took a sentence to compose a seven-character quatrain. Moreover, since we are meeting the movie queen and advocating saving the country through dancing, we cannot but write a poem to promote it. Last year, the newspaper reported that Mr. Xiong Xiling traveled to West Lake and filled in the "Nian Nu Jiao" lyrics, saying:

The afterglow of the twin peaks, watching the towers and pavilions vying to rise, thousands of households. I sigh that the people of the southeast are exhausted, and the lake and mountains are still singing and dancing. Hearing the Jiangchao from afar, the Xutao roars, all for private feuds. Only the lone cypress stands tall, loyal for thousands of years. I remember the monarchs and ministers of Goujian, lying on firewood and tasting gall, persevering to preserve the territory. An unparalleled beauty can help the country, shaming countless men. The enemy's power is spreading, the court disputes have not stopped, and the Jin soldiers are crossing again. Where is the national soul? Who is the master in the territory today?

Mr. Xiong is, after all, an old man, and his attitude is serious. Although he fills in the old tune of stringed instruments and debauchery, he also contains the solitary feelings of sorrow and concern for the country. If it were a young man, engaged in the "lyrical liberation movement," what is said in the lyrics would be nothing more than "playing mahjong," "minding his own business," and "[expletive] about the country!"

Carrot Hair 178

— Written by Jules Kenaro, Translated by Lin Qu

Agathe

Replacing Ololine was Agathe, a daughter related to Ololine. Carrot Hair observed the new maid with great curiosity. Within a few days, the Lepic family had shifted their attention from Carrot Hair to the new maid. "Agathe," said the Lepic family, "you should knock on the door before entering a room, but that doesn't mean you have to kick the door through with your hooves like a horse." "She's taken office," thought Carrot Hair, "but let's see how she behaves at mealtime." Everyone gathered in the spacious kitchen to eat. Agathe had a napkin draped over her arm, ready to run from that side to the sideboard, from the sideboard to the dining table, because she didn't know how to walk properly, she would rather run panting, her cheeks flushed. She spoke too fast, laughed too loudly, and wanted to work too hard. Mr. Lepic sat down first, unfolded his napkin, pushed his plate next to the dish in front of him, took some meat and gravy, and dragged the plate back. He poured his own drink, hunched his back, lowered his eyes, and ate carefully, as listless as usual. When changing dishes, he would lower his head, look at the chair, and shift his buttocks. Mrs. Lepic personally divided the food for her children, first for the eldest brother, Felix, because he was shouting that he was hungry, then for the eldest daughter, Eleestine, because she was older, and finally for Carrot Hair, who was sitting at the end of the table. He never asked for more food, as if this was normally forbidden. One portion should be enough for him, and if others gave him more, he would accept it. He didn't drink water, and he filled his mouth with food that he didn't like, just to please Mrs. Lepic, because she was the only one in the family who liked to eat. The eldest brother, Felix, and the eldest daughter, Eleestine, were more free. They finished one portion and wanted a second portion. They followed Mr. Lepic's method and pushed the plate next to the dish for serving. But no one spoke. "What's wrong with them?" thought Agathe. But nothing was wrong with them. They just didn't talk, that's all. She really couldn't help but stretch out her arms and yawn at this family. Mr. Lepic ate slowly, as if chewing on broken glass. Although Mrs. Lepic was normally as talkative as a magpie, at the dining table, she would only use her hands and head to gesture and direct everything. The eldest daughter, Eleestine, raised her eyes and looked at the ceiling. The eldest brother, Felix, played with bread crumbs. Carrot Hair, who didn't have a water glass, only paid attention to when to use bread to wipe his plate clean. He wiped it too quickly, fearing that others would say he was greedy, and wiped it too late, fearing that others would say he was slow. Therefore, he engaged in complicated calculations. Suddenly, Mr. Lepic took the water bottle on the dining table and poured a full bottle of clear water. "I can do this too," said Agathe. No, she didn't say it, she just thought it. She was also infected by them, and her tongue became numb. She didn't dare to speak, but she thought that it was her fault for letting the master pour the water himself, so she became extra careful. (To be continued)

Economic Special Issue 179

Issue 22 (Published every Monday)

Over ninety years of importing foreign goods, tens of millions of taels of export indemnities, and over twenty years of incessant internal strife and rural bankruptcy, are still only half of the truth. The reality is that the people are impoverished and the wealth is exhausted, and the entire social economy is on the verge of collapse. As for how to revitalize the countryside, neither high-sounding discussions can be effective, nor can extravagant exposition of academic theories and collection of established rules be helpful. As Mr. Sun Yat-sen said, "Follow our own social situation and meet the world's trends." What is urgently needed now is to solve how the stagnant money in the cities can flow into the hands of the farmers, how the farmers' products can come to the cities, and how to give farmers the opportunity to recuperate, the wish for a well-off family, and to achieve the goal of enriching the people. In a word, construction that can be delayed but must not be neglected, and allowing the people to rest. Stop the oppressive exactions of taxes and pass on the nurturing of life. The cooperative system can indeed be emulated, but we should consider the farmers' level of knowledge and the prejudices of public and private economies. Can they be transferred? Oranges become trifoliate oranges when they cross the Huai River, let alone the transplantation of all systems? Therefore, the most practical and easy to implement at present is to reform, revise, and promote the existing system. For example, organizing agricultural loans, facilitating low-interest funds and pawnshops, and assisting farmers' gatherings (silver money associations) to engage in production can all make up for the shortcomings of farmers' banks. As for usury, it is indeed a distant cause of rural bankruptcy. We must know that the reason for usury is originally a social pathology. If farmers have ample economies and financial organizations are perfect, how can usury occur? At present, what makes farmers feel even more difficult is precisely the inability to obtain usury. Most of the usurers in rural areas are only one room away from poor farmers. Those who are more substantial, seeing the current situation, dare not lend even if they have money, and instead move cash to the cities to prevent any danger. As a result, the number of chips in the countryside becomes less and less, and the turnover becomes less and less flexible, which brews today's phenomenon. Therefore, the measure to treat the symptoms is still to appeal to the local wealthy households with righteousness and profit, and to give them corresponding guarantees, to persuade them to invest in loans, to appropriately reduce interest rates, or to purchase agricultural products that cannot be stored, in order to broaden the farmers' livelihood. In this issue, we have the honor of receiving masterpieces from Mr. Xu Shuji, Mr. Huang Gutong, Mr. Tang Huizun, and Mr. Huang Tong, all of which are works that combine learning and experience, and cannot be compared with those who simply talk emptily. In addition, we are grateful for the contributions of our readers. Due to space limitations, we cannot prepare for war. We apologize for this. Liu Tang

Rural Revitalization and the Relationship with Farmers 180

Xu Xuan

Two Major Premises for Establishing Agricultural Policy

In recent years, the cry of "rural bankruptcy" has been rampant in our country. As a result, the so-called agricultural relief plans have sprung up like mushrooms after rain, appearing in words and scattered in newspapers. The government has also gradually paid attention to this, such as the food conferences, agricultural finance conferences, and silk relief conferences, which have been heard from time to time. Recently, the Executive Yuan has even established an Agricultural Revitalization Committee to convene colleagues from all over the country to discuss with each other. Although its contents are not detailed, according to the reports in the newspapers, its general outline can already be seen. Whether it can be actually implemented in the future, or to what extent it can be implemented, I dare not predict now. What is most expected is that no matter what kind of plan or what kind of facilities, they must be based on the farmers. Otherwise, the name of a policy, although sufficient to call for a moment, is not actually the case, or it is counterproductive. Although it comes out of the rural revitalization, I am afraid that the long clothes will be slow, and I do not know when I will see the white of the East.

At present, the agricultural situation in our country is gradually declining. It is certainly necessary to establish various agricultural policies to improve it. However, agriculture cannot improve itself. Those who engage in agriculture are farmers. If we do not first maintain and stabilize the farmers' lives, and want them to improve agriculture with a body that is tired all day long and cannot get enough to eat, can they do it? The rural areas of our country have always been the source of national wealth and the foundation of society. In recent years, the signs of decline have increased with themselves. We must quickly seek revitalization. However, the rural areas cannot revitalize themselves. Those who organize the rural areas are farmers. If we do not first improve the economic conditions of the farmers, so that they can live and work in peace and contentment, and do not see the differences and move away from their hometowns, and want the prosperity of the rural areas, it is also like climbing trees to catch fish. Therefore, if we want to determine or implement agricultural policies or rural revitalization plans, we must always and everywhere focus on the farmers.

Originally, agricultural problems or rural problems have close relationships with politics, economics, education, and all social problems. Therefore, farmers are often dominated by politics, economics, education, and social systems. Therefore, if we want to discuss the relationship between rural revitalization and farmers, the scope involved is very broad and large. Due to space limitations, I cannot describe them one by one. I will just briefly list a few examples from the rural areas themselves to show the necessity of a farmer-based policy.

The great disease of the current rural areas can be summed up in the word "poverty." Therefore, if we want to cure the disease of the rural areas, we must first save the poverty of the rural areas. However, the rural areas are not poor by themselves. The poverty of the farmers who live in the rural areas makes them poor. The way to save poverty is that agricultural financial policy is still the same. However, if this policy is not based on the farmers, its effect will be minimal. In the current Chinese agricultural financial institutions, there are only a few agricultural stars. Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces are slightly better, but the circulation of agricultural funds is still limited. In the future, agricultural financial institutions should be greatly expanded so that urban finance and rural finance can regulate each other to eliminate the evils of urban expansion and rural decline. However, if we only follow the beautiful name of agricultural finance, and do not consider the interests of the farmers themselves, then the poverty of the farmers is still the same, and the poverty of the rural areas is also the same! For example, the farmers' bank lends money to the farmers so that they can avoid the exploitation of usury. Its intention is very good. However, the amount of benefits the farmers receive still depends on its lending conditions. In terms of the amount of money, the farmers want more and more, but the bank is afraid that the money will be recovered, and it will not give it. The two have their own reasons and cannot be blamed. However, since the farmers want to borrow money to engage in agriculture, if they are honest and trustworthy, the bank should supply it as much as possible. Otherwise, if the farmers borrow 1,000 yuan, the bank only lends 500 yuan, or less than this amount, then the farmers' business plan is broken, although it is better than "one text is not known," but the benefits are very small. In terms of guarantees, small farmers generally have no land and lack credit, so it is difficult to borrow money like climbing to the sky. Even if the bank promises to borrow money on credit, it often asks them to find substantial shops to guarantee before they are willing to lend money. If the farmers can get substantial shops to guarantee them, then their credit is enough to borrow money from other places, why bother begging the bank? He often spends several days trying to find a shop guarantee, but in the end, he cannot find it, and he returns disappointed. Or he has to travel a long distance, which increases the loss. It is very pitiful. In terms of the time limit, agricultural loans should be compatible with the nature of agriculture. To purchase seeds and mulberry leaves, if the time limit is too short, they must be sold cheaply after redemption to repay the debt. How can the farmers benefit from the small amount of harvest? From this point of view, agricultural finance is a good policy for revitalizing the rural areas, but if the loans are not considered for the farmers, then the farmers will not be able to enjoy its actual benefits, so as to improve their economic conditions, and its effect will be minimal. "Backward production" is also the most serious problem in the current rural areas. It seems that encouraging the increase in production cannot be delayed. However, if the production policy is not supported by the price adjustment policy, when production is insufficient, both producers and consumers will suffer; when there is a surplus, consumers may not benefit, and producers may be trapped. For example, the demand for rice is inelastic. Even if the price of rice falls sharply, consumers cannot eat a few more liters of rice every day to the point of being full. If producers are forced to sell each other after the autumn harvest due to the economy, then the price of rice will inevitably fall sharply at one time, which is not enough to compensate for their production costs, and they will be even more embarrassed. The "bumper harvest becoming a disaster" of rice last year is a clear proof of this. Last year, although the rice fields in various provinces were not a great harvest, in recent years, it can be considered a relatively bumper harvest. It is appropriate for production to increase, and the farmers all held their hands in gratitude. However, the facts are the opposite. The price of rice has fallen sharply. The reasons are very complicated, and its impact is also serious in all aspects. People from all walks of life have shouted loudly, all using the term "raising the price of rice." The Ministry of Finance also convened a food conference to seek relief. Not to mention that the policies they proposed have not yet been implemented, even if they are implemented, saving the price of rice may not be of much benefit to the farmers. Most of the farmers have already sold the rice after the autumn harvest, and even if there is surplus grain, the number is very small. Therefore, the price adjustment policy for rice should be considered for the farmers in advance, and ways should be found to maintain its price before the price of rice falls. In this way, the farmers can enjoy the benefits of increased rice production. Otherwise, if we wait until the price of rice falls sharply, and the farmers have no surplus grain, and then begin to seek ways to raise the price of rice in a panic, then when the price of rice falls sharply, the farmers have suffered from the low price of rice. Once the price of rice gradually rises in the spring and summer of the following year, the farmers have to buy rice to fill their hunger, and they suffer from the high price of rice. Therefore, the price adjustment policy for rice, although it is a good method, if it is not based on the farmers and used at the right time, then the farmers will still find it difficult to enjoy the benefits of increased rice production. Not only rice, but also the relationship between the production and price of other agricultural products is the same. Therefore, the production policy and the price adjustment policy should be considered at the same time and adapted to local conditions, so that the price of agricultural products will be stabilized, and the farmers can enjoy the real benefits of increased production. In this way, the economic status of the farmers will be higher day by day, and the rural areas will also prosper accordingly.

The above is only a few points, but from this, it can be seen that agricultural policies and rural revitalization plans must be based on the farmers in order to have any effect. Otherwise, the farmers will be subjected to various oppressions and will not be able to survive. To expect the agriculture operated by the farmers to gradually develop, and the rural areas composed of the farmers to improve day by day, is like asking a cripple to lift a thousand pounds or a lame person to chase a running rabbit. I know that it is impossible. The farmers in our country today are extremely exhausted and are almost without a voice. If we can catch up, support them, and motivate them, so that they can focus on farming and be happy, and so that the strong will not become bandits and the weak will not turn into ditches, then it is not too late to mend the fold after the sheep is lost. If we continue to delay the time, and there are policies that cannot be implemented, or they are implemented in the wrong way, I am afraid that in a few years, the farmers will be on the verge of extinction, and agriculture will be lost forever! Can the future of the country bear to say it? May 10, 20

Rural Revitalization Issues 181

Huang Kutong

In the midst of frequent alarms of war and a grave national crisis, the Executive Yuan established the Rural Revitalization Committee. The Yuan invited prominent figures from various fields, held a two-day meeting, and resolved many important matters. It also decided that branch committees should be established in various provinces to undertake investigations, construction, and implementation. It is expected that the work on rural revitalization will be intensified, and the decline of the rural areas will be reversed. This is a matter worthy of celebration.

The detailed content of the matters resolved at the meeting is not yet fully known. However, based on newspaper reports, I do not find any particularly novel strategies. As the saying goes, "There is nothing new under the sun." In the end, it is just rehashing old tunes. For example, the items related to technology, economy, and rural self-governance are mostly things that many central meetings have discussed before (although the names and programs may be different). However, rehashing old tunes is not a mistake but rather indicates that the issue is becoming increasingly profound. Therefore, one should not suppress the rehashing of old tunes, but rather worry about the forgetting of old tunes.

In recent years, there have been many calls regarding the collapse of rural areas, the suffering of farmers, and the agricultural panic, as well as records of these facts. There is no need to repeat them here. However, we must pay attention to the fact that the collapse of rural areas, the suffering of farmers, and the agricultural panic are not localized or individual issues of rural areas, farmers, or agriculture. Instead, they are nurtured and generated by the functions of the entire political and economic system, as well as feudal forces. This is the so-called internal cause. We must also pay attention to the role of imperialism in colonizing China. This is the so-called external cause. These two causes are intertwined to deplete the vitality, and the rural areas have long been in decline, showing chronic symptoms since at least the Opium War. Since the founding of the Republic, the chronic symptoms have become acute and increasingly profound. In other words, rural areas are not just collapsing, but bankrupt; farmers are not just suffering, but fleeing; agriculture is not just panicking, but failing. If these internal and external causes cannot be resolved, the so-called rural revitalization will ultimately be like quenching thirst with plums or skimming boiling water. Therefore, our first concept should be to eliminate harm, with promoting benefits being secondary. For example, if a person has been sick for a long time and their internal organs are failing, if the doctor does not first use medicine or perform surgery to cleanse the organs and suddenly gives them tonics like ginseng and deer antler, it will not only be useless but may even kill them! The principle of eliminating harm before promoting benefits is the same. Regarding external causes, only by implementing anti-imperialist work can they be resolved. This will not be discussed here for now. As for internal causes, they are the so-called internal affairs issues, which are also a prerequisite for rural revitalization. In other words, the work of eliminating harm is to first implement a passive agricultural policy. In my personal opinion, there are several things that must be resolved first. Briefly stated, they are: ㈠ rural security; ㈡ the high pressure of land taxes; ㈢ the exploitation of usury; ㈣ the exploitation of tenant rents; ㈤ the forced allocation of public bonds; ㈥ the conscription of soldiers and corvée labor; ㈦ exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies; ㈧ opium and gambling; and ㈨ natural disasters. I believe that it is necessary to resolve these nine matters first. However, to resolve these, it is necessary to first break the feudal forces of warlords, bureaucrats, and local bullies. Otherwise, if one drives away the tiger from the front door, a wolf will enter through the back door. The rural areas will still not prosper. As for the suppression of the communists, the government is working hard on it, so there is no need to mention it.

Humble Opinions on Rural Revitalization 182

Tang Hui-sun

At a time when our country is plagued by disasters and the people are struggling to survive, the authorities are cautiously advocating rural revitalization as the fundamental plan to save the country. Our country is known as an agricultural country, with agricultural population accounting for eight out of ten. The country's financial resources are mostly derived from rural areas. Nineteen of the foreign trade are agricultural products. Therefore, the fact that the lifeblood of our country's politics and economy today depends on agriculture is also evident. The decline of rural areas and the panic of agriculture have swept the world, and it is not unique to our country. However, after investigating the underlying causes, the agricultural panic in our country is definitely not comparable to the agricultural panic in Europe and America. The agricultural panic in Europe and America is largely due to the development of agricultural technology and overproduction, which are mostly internal causes of agriculture. The agricultural panic in our country is largely due to the internal causes of semi-feudal production relations, such as military disasters, banditry, exorbitant taxes, and heavy labor. Understanding this, the decline of rural areas and the panic of agriculture in our country cannot be compared to the agricultural panic in Europe and America, which are considered purely economic problems. The Rural Revitalization Committee gathered prominent figures in the country to discuss ways to revitalize rural areas. Technology, economy, and organization, various resolutions, are all necessary conditions for rural revitalization. Most of them are proposals that have been made in various central meetings in the past but have not been implemented. If the central government has the sincerity and determination to revitalize the rural areas and can implement these resolutions step by step, the revitalization of the rural areas can be expected soon.

Furthermore, the decline of rural areas and the panic of agriculture in our country are due to both internal and external causes. If we only start with the internal improvement of agriculture and the efforts of the farmers themselves to revitalize rural areas, while the political situation remains the same, the disasters of soldiers and bandits are not reduced, and the poor production relations remain the same, then even if agriculture improves and farmers free themselves, the decline of rural areas and the panic of agriculture will not be improved. I make this argument not because I think the methods resolved by the Rural Revitalization Committee are not good. The methods resolved by the Rural Revitalization Committee, which are to improve the problems of the rural areas themselves, are indeed perfect. However, whether they can be implemented and achieve practical results depends only on the improvement of politics in the future, the stability of the local areas, and the implementation of all social policies. Otherwise, the so-called rural revitalization is only equivalent to empty talk on paper and is no different from the various meetings convened by the central government in the past, which were discussed but could not be implemented.

Today, discussions on rural issues are nothing more than the two aspects of agricultural business and farmers' lives. The decline of rural areas is also constituted by the two major causes of the decline of agricultural business and the poverty of farmers' lives. The focus of the decline of agricultural business is the poor production relations. The poverty of farmers' lives is due to the low level of farmers' knowledge. Therefore, to revitalize rural areas, we should first pay attention to these two points. Most of the farmers in our country are small farmers. The area of cultivated land per household is not even enough to distribute the labor of the family. Even if all the income belongs to them, it is not enough for their livelihood. Moreover, a large part of it must be paid for rent and exorbitant taxes. How can we expect farmers not to be poor and rural areas not to decline? This is like climbing a tree to catch fish, how can it be possible? Therefore, I say that if we do not want to revitalize rural areas, then so be it. If we want to revitalize rural areas, we must first change the agricultural production relations, implement land policies, and realize Mr. Sun Yat-sen's advocacy of equal land rights and the tiller owning his land. Once the production relations are changed and the area of cultivated land per household is expanded, the agricultural labor can be rationally allocated, and agricultural technology can be adopted. As a result, production increases and income is abundant, and the problems of agricultural business can be solved.

Education in our country is mostly biased towards cities. Even in the developed areas of education in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, the so-called rural education is still far from being universal. No wonder the villagers are ignorant and at the mercy of others, and all the undertakings in the rural areas are controlled by a small number of local bullies and ruffians. The poverty of farmers' lives is caused by the ignorance of farmers' knowledge, which prevents them from forming self-help and mutual-aid organizations. Therefore, to improve farmers' lives and promote rural autonomy, we should first popularize rural education to increase farmers' knowledge, which is a crucial plan. In recent years, our country has been vigorously promoting agricultural cooperation, and the Rural Revitalization Committee has also paid attention to this point. The cooperative system can regulate rural finance and increase farmers' production. The method is good and the intention is beautiful, and it should be promoted extensively to be established throughout the rural areas of our country, which is also an important item for rural revitalization. However, the cooperative system

takes the spirit of self-help and mutual aid, and the key is that "everyone is for me, and I am for everyone." Therefore, it is easy to promote cooperative enterprises, but it is difficult to make them succeed. Denmark is known as the world's model agricultural country. Its agricultural development is due to the success of the cooperative system. The success of the cooperative system depends entirely on the foundation of rural education as its precursor. Finally, I would like to add one more point, which is about the issue of rural financial relief. The Rural Revitalization Committee has definite methods for rural financial relief. It has also requested the Shanghai Banking Association to initiate the establishment of a Rural Financial Adjustment Committee to assist in the adjustment of rural finance. If it can be implemented, the benefits to the villagers will be significant. I believe that the adjustment of agricultural finance lies in the ability to transfer the finance concentrated in the cities to the rural areas. So that the finance of a country can circulate and turn around like the circulation of blood, and not stagnate and wither. Therefore, the establishment of rural financial institutions must be based on this intention. However, at present, the Farmers Bank and Agricultural and Industrial Bank in various provinces of our country are still established in large cities. They cannot directly lend to farmers, nor can they transfer their funds to the local areas to achieve financial decentralization, which loses the fundamental purpose of rural financial decentralization. I believe that the current agricultural financial institutions in our country must strive to decentralize and spread to remote rural areas, so that even if their funds are small, the villagers can still get the real benefits of financial accommodation. Otherwise, although we talk about adjusting rural finance, it is just enough to promote the concentration of finance in the cities. This is also a point that should be noted in rural revitalization. The above mentioned are plain and unremarkable, and inevitably old-fashioned. However, if they can be implemented one by one, the benefits to our farmers will not be small.

Although the rural areas of China have been subjected to imperialist aggression for a long time, their core is still dominated by feudal forces. The production relations in rural areas are still feudal and dominated by land. Therefore, the land issue is a serious issue that must be resolved. Most of the farmers in China do not have land, and those who do have very little (the average area per household is less than thirty mu).

In this way, new farming methods and new technologies cannot be promoted, the means of production cannot be changed, the productive forces cannot be increased, and the rural economy cannot be enriched. Therefore, I believe that from a positive policy perspective, we should first change the current production relations in rural areas. However, given the current situation, changing the production relations in rural areas is easier said than done. If we can achieve the so-called "the tiller owns his land," it would already be a remarkable achievement. In short, what is most hoped for now is to implement a passive agricultural policy, which is to achieve the work of eliminating harm. In the old-fashioned way, it is hoped that we can soothe and recuperate the people, and in the new terminology, it is to implement the liberation of farmers. Otherwise, every time we take an action, the farmers will suffer one more point of pain. As the saying goes, "Three more things to erect a spirit tablet means more ghosts." This is not because the policy itself is bad, but because of the relationship between the root and the branch. Furthermore, based on the facts, those who implement policies often abuse their power for personal gain and use the name of new policies to carry out extortion. Farmers not only have no power to accept it but are also frightened by it. If the new things are not based on the objective situation but are created behind closed doors, it will be even worse, and the majority of farmers will be sacrificed. Or, if it is handled too eagerly and without regard to the interests of the farmers, it will cause trouble. Therefore, it is not only wrong to intentionally harm the government, but it is also impossible to cut one's feet to fit the shoes. What do farmers need most now? In my opinion, the first is to need peace and to eliminate all kinds of oppression and exploitation. Therefore, if we can eliminate harm for the farmers, it will be equivalent to stimulating their function of promoting benefits. Shanghai has accumulated a large amount of cash, which indicates the fact that rural areas are bankrupt and the interior finance is exhausted. Therefore, this time the Rural Revitalization Committee resolved to "request the Shanghai Banking Association to initiate the establishment of a Rural Financial Adjustment Committee, and the banks will jointly or freely do their best to assist in the adjustment of rural finance." Since last year, the sound of banks in Shanghai lending money to save agriculture has been loud.

But how much money has been actually lent out and how many farmers have been saved? After this meeting, it is expected that the bankers will be able to make further efforts, and the majority of farmers who are struggling to survive are waiting for the arrival of the god of wealth.

The establishment of any policy should be based on objective facts, and the implementation of policies requires the concerted efforts of the government, public and private organizations, individuals, and other parties in order to achieve success. Furthermore, there should be a specialized agency to conduct continuous research and expose the objective facts without reservation as the basis for establishing policies, so as to avoid the problem of building a car behind closed doors and not being able to fit the tracks when going out. After the establishment of the Rural Revitalization Committee this time, it is hoped that it can truly and practically implement the work of revitalizing rural areas. What will be the results in the future? Helpless farmers are waiting for the elixir to revive them!

I have said some nonsense above, and the planned number of words has been reached, so I will submit the paper. (May 9, 22nd year of the Republic)

Revitalizing Rural Areas and the Issue of Agricultural Usury 183

Huang Tong

I.

Everyone knows that the collapse of agriculture and rural bankruptcy are the most serious problems in China today. Because China's current economic stage is still stagnant in a small-scale agricultural economy, "Agriculture is the foundation of the world and the people depend on it for their livelihood; if the foundation is not solid, the country will not be stable." This old-fashioned saying is still very applicable now! The Executive Yuan invited contemporary celebrities and experts to hold a meeting on revitalizing rural areas in the capital on the 5th and 6th of this month and passed many programs. This is indeed a grand event worthy of our excitement! However, how can rural areas be revitalized? The most important thing is to prevent farmers from escaping the villages and to make them live and work in peace and contentment. To make farmers live and work in peace and contentment, it is especially important to eliminate the relations of production of exploitation and being exploited in the rural areas. Of course, the implementation of Mr. Sun Yat-sen's legacy, "The tiller should have his land," is a prerequisite and fundamental condition for revitalizing rural areas. The scope of this issue is very large, and there is no time to discuss it in detail here. Now, let me briefly mention the situation of agricultural usury to glimpse a small part of the exploitative relations in rural areas. II.

Usury is when lenders use their economically strong position to exploit borrowers through heavy interest rates to achieve the purpose of exploitation. In other words, it is the exploitation of heavy interest rates. Under the current private property system, there are rich people who "own tens of thousands of yi" on one side and poor households who "have nothing but bare walls" on the other. Exploitation of heavy interest rates exists everywhere, and it is not limited to rural areas. However, rural areas are particularly brutal due to various special reasons. The rampant usury in rural areas is due to the difficulties in rural finance. There are many reasons for the lack of capital in rural areas, the most important of which is the accelerated concentration of capital in cities. In recent years, the surge in bank savings and cash reserves in various commercial ports has been almost the same. Shanghai is the most prominent. The silver reserves in Shanghai in November of the 21st year of the Republic were only 57,899,000 taels, but by January of this year (22nd year of the Republic), they had increased to 144,959,000 taels, more than doubling. The silver dollar reserves in March of the 20th year of the Republic were 13,379,000 yuan, but by January of this year, they had increased to 22,417,000 yuan, more than doubling. The phenomenon of cash accumulation can be seen (see Yang Yin-pu's "Urban Finance and Rural Finance in China," New China, Volume 1, Issue 8). Recently, the daily increase in the exchange rate of copper coins, how can we know that it is not because the rural areas are short of silver and are sending copper coins out?

On the other hand, in rural areas, farmers' savings are being depleted more and more. The savings of middle-class farmers do not exceed ten or twenty yuan, and some even cannot find one yuan in cash (see the Bank of China's Business Report for the 21st year of the Republic)! Seen from the countryside, farmers cannot find a few copper coins. The "money shortage" in rural areas has reached such a degree that the rampant usury and the intensification of its exploitation are "inevitable." III. The forms of usury in rural areas can be generally divided into four types: money, livestock, land, and goods. ㈠ Money Usury: In addition to lending money at very high interest rates, there are also cases where the interest rate is normal, but the principal is discounted when the money is initially delivered; or a note is made for an amount higher than the actual amount borrowed, and the borrower is required to repay the full amount later. In addition, taking advantage of the poverty of farmers to buy their beneficial claims against third parties at very low prices is also a type of money usury. ㈡ Livestock Usury: When farmers with less capital lose their livestock and cannot afford to buy them again, their distress is used to lend them livestock for raising. After a certain period, usually after the livestock gives birth, the total number or price of the livestock is divided equally between the two parties; or the lender gets the young livestock, and the borrower gets the mother livestock. This method may seem innocent on the surface; however, livestock merchants often take advantage of this loan contract to overestimate the price of the livestock at the time of lending and underestimate it at the time of distribution, thereby taking excessive profits. Livestock merchants are superior in capital and often control the monopoly of buying and selling in a locality, thereby manipulating market prices, so their harm to farmers may not be second to anyone. ㈢ Land Usury: When small and medium-sized farmers or hired laborers are eager to obtain land, they sell their land at very high prices; or they lend their land at very high rents to reap huge profits. ㈣ Goods Usury: This mostly occurs when farmers and debtors have a debt relationship. For example, the farmers' produce is estimated at a low price to offset the principal and interest; or cheap goods are sold to farmers at high prices, all of which are their usual tricks. Among the above four types, money usury is the most common, followed by livestock usury and goods usury, and land usury is relatively rare. These four types have no clear boundaries, and there are many names for them, too many to list.

IV. The evils of usury have long been recognized by the general public, especially in rural areas. As a result of rampant usury, self-cultivating farmers are reduced to tenant farmers, then to hired laborers, and then to unemployed people. Driven by hunger and cold, they take risks, and then gather in the mountains and forests to kill and rob, eventually becoming a major scourge to the country (the rise and fall of a part of the Twenty-Four Histories are all like this)! No one is born to be fond of making trouble. In recent years, bandits have been everywhere, and violence has been rampant, most of which are caused by the environment. To eliminate evil fruits, we must first eliminate evil causes. Therefore, the crackdown on usury is urgent! The methods of combating usury are nothing more than two: the passive one is to stipulate the highest interest rate by the state and use the law to enforce it; the active one is to establish agricultural financial institutions to facilitate the flow of capital. If there is only passive resistance, it will never be able to eliminate it, why? Because under the social system of profit-seeking, it is a very natural fact that capital generates interest; and the level of interest rates is inextricably linked to the prosperity and decline of enterprises and the abundance or shortage of capital, which cannot be controlled by an order or a mere scrap of paper. In the past, political economists with ethical ideas invariably opposed lending capital for interest. The philosopher Aristotle even advocated the theory of non-fecundity of money (Baerten theory of mcney), meaning that money is a medium of exchange, and its intrinsic value cannot generate any wealth, so lending money for interest is extremely improper. The medieval scholastic philosophers (Scholagtiker)

and canonists (canonis) believed that wealthy lenders charging interest to poor borrowers was contrary to God's command and also advocated prohibition. However, due to practical necessity, they gradually learned about the convenience of it! Canon law (anonlaw) records three exceptions: namely, the property owner's claim for compensation for losses suffered due to lending (DamnuMEmergens), the claim for compensation for lost profits (lucram cssans) due to lending, and the claim for compensation for risks incurred due to lending (Perlculam sortis) are not regarded as interest and are considered legitimate rights. Secondly, regarding the statutory interest rate, predecessors also advocated it. For example, the Englishman Josiah Child in the 17th century admired the wealth and power of the Netherlands and vigorously advocated the statutory interest rate, believing that the wealth and power of the Netherlands was due to the low interest rate; the level of interest rates was not based on external natural conditions, but the government could freely decide with public power, so if the government wanted to enrich the country and benefit the people, the first thing it had to do was to use its power to limit the market interest rate. However, what is the reality? In the 16th year of the Republic, the 111th Central Political Conference of the Kuomintang resolved that the maximum annual interest rate should not exceed 20% and issued an order to the whole country to comply with it. However, facts tell us that the creditors under the rule of the National Government still exploited heavy interest rates as before, and even disobeyed the law and intensified their efforts. For example, in order to avoid conflict with the law, they first added the interest to the principal, or deducted the interest in advance, and wrote on the contract the words "borrowed a certain amount of money, with an annual interest rate of "one point"." In this way, even if the government wants to crack down, it cannot start! As mentioned above, under the current social system of private property, interest and interest rates cannot be prohibited or restricted by simply issuing an order, which is already clear. Then, the crackdown on usury must seek another active method, which is to establish agricultural financial institutions. In our country, the existing rural financial institutions include money shops, pawnshops, and mutual aid societies; the emerging ones include agricultural banks and rural credit cooperatives, etc., which also have a considerable number. However, the existing ones are gradually declining and mostly transformed into tools for exploiting farmers; the emerging ones are mostly nominal and have weak strength. It can be said that there are "absolutely none" that can truly facilitate agricultural credit and provide assistance to rural areas!

This time, the Rural Revitalization Committee passed the outline proposed by the Economic Group, in which, regarding rural economic issues, it advocated the establishment of a farmers' bank in each province in addition to cooperatives, with branches established in various places in the province, and the establishment of agricultural warehouses in various counties; at the same time, the existing pawnshops in various places should still be supported by the provinces to the best of their ability. On the one hand, it has requested the Shanghai Banking Association to initiate the establishment of a Rural Financial Adjustment Committee to do its best to assist in the adjustment of rural finance. It can be said that "the key is raised and the mesh is stretched, without missing a single detail"! If it can be actively promoted, the dilapidated and dying rural areas may have hope of revitalization! (May 10, 22nd year of the Republic)

Discussions

Luck and Laziness 187

— Tian Fang

Recently, flower clubs have flourished, bringing booming business to pawnshops and Buddhist temples, with the middle and lower classes being the most addicted, especially women and workers. This is indeed a very serious social problem. Gambling is said to be most prevalent in America, where even a presidential election involves betting. However, it is even more common in China. Whether it's the points on a card, the number of copper coins in hand, or even whether it will be sunny or rainy tomorrow, or whether a newborn child is male or female, everything can be bet on. Mahjong is even known as the "national game." In short, everything in the hands of the Chinese becomes gambling material. Gambling is essentially an immature psychology, linked to luck and laziness, which is a social pathology. Those who rely on luck are unwilling to work diligently and practically, always hoping for instant success and immense profits. In business, they expect others to support them; in earning money, they dream of winning the lottery, unwilling to make their own efforts, fantasizing about unexpected encounters. If they suffer a loss, instead of seeking help from others, they hope for natural disasters to befall the other party. This is truly an unhealthy and decadent phenomenon, yet it is prevalent today among both the government and the common people. The government seeks to make a windfall, such as by increasing taxes and soliciting donations instead of developing real industries, which is the same principle as the common people playing flower clubs. The foundation for this pathology is laziness. Lazy people's behavior and thoughts are inversely proportional. The lazier their behavior, the more fanciful their thoughts. Because they lack practical ability, they seek fulfillment in fantasy. Those who dream of becoming immortals or Buddhas to save the world are unwilling to put in even a little effort into producing food and clothing for the present world, which is clear evidence of this. Therefore, instant success is merely the delusion of fools, and undeserved gains and unexpected requests are only hoped for by lazy people, and gambling is a manifestation of this inferior nature. Sound-minded people only know to accumulate little by little and work steadfastly, without dreaming of ascending to heaven in one step. However, how many sound-minded people are there? The transformation of national psychology still requires effort.

Resisting Donations 188

— Chang

"Judging from the newspaper, the students are going to solicit donations along the road again. But we have to leave early and return late. If we run into them, we're not happy to give money, but we also feel embarrassed not to. It's really annoying." Our warehouse supervisor, the burly Lao Cao, held a copy of Shen Bao and muttered resentfully.

"I have a solution! As long as one of us donates one yuan, gets a badge, and we all use it, we can pass without hindrance. If we divide it among our sixteen colleagues, each person only pays six fen and two and a half li. Wouldn't that be cheaper and nicer?" The opium addict Lao Chen shrugged his shoulders and devised this plan.

"No! No! The last time I encountered these students asking for donations on the road, I deliberately asked them how much they needed. They said with a smile, 'Whatever you want.' So I solemnly took out a copper coin and gave it to them. Although they were angry, they couldn't do anything because they had said 'whatever you want.' Haha! How satisfying is that? Six fen and two and a half li is enough to eat ten more soup dumplings." Lao Cao said triumphantly.

"Hmm..."

"Right..."

"Gentlemen, dinner is ready!" The tea boy A Gen shouted, and everyone scattered.

This is an informal meeting record from our factory yesterday after the afternoon work and before dinner. Lao Cao and Lao Chen are originally Laurel and Hardy in our factory. Recently, they have also been appointed as the secretaries of the Deputy King of Hell, so the plans they come up with are always superior. I hope all readers of the newspaper will learn from their cleverness, so that the benevolent and righteous Japanese will come to Shanghai and treat us to a feast.

Shanghai Ways 190

— Fen

The reputation, making a living.

Shanghai is a hell on earth, filled with a menacing and uneasy atmosphere. Every trade has its own path, and there are ways for loafers, hooligans, petty thugs, show-offs, and prostitutes. As long as you open your eyes and observe, there are endless mysteries. At the corners of the streets and in amusement parks, you can often see loafing friends squaring off like fighting roosters. If you provoke their anger, they will tilt their heads, stare with triangular eyes, and shout:

"Who is your leader?"

This way, he is telling you that he has his superior, his leader (not a committee member or the mayor, but his brother). He wants to know if you know your place. An experienced friend, without showing weakness, will inquire about his "leader." Or, if a fight breaks out, don't be afraid, he will say, "Let's go to the Qinglian Pavilion for a chat, meet some friends." This is his "leader." Change the approach, beg for mercy. This is no small matter, roll up your sleeves, raise what seems like his unique bare fists, and change his tone:

"Calling you to make a living!"

In this case, you'd better be calm and ready to fight. Watch his movements. If you have strength, you might as well strike first and let him taste your living. At this time, someone claiming to be "one of us" will come out to mediate. You can let go and say a few words:

"We're all one of us, let's just let it go!"

There are many tricks like this, but I haven't tried these tricks. Coming to Shanghai forever, there will always be a chance to taste something fresher!

Entanglements in Dissolving the Engagement of a Child Bride 191

Editor:

My younger sister is twenty-one years old this year. She was betrothed to a farmer in the same village when she was young. When she was nine years old, because my mother passed away, and my father and I were both working elsewhere, my uncle (the matchmaker) took my sister to the other family as a child bride without permission. Who knew that her in-laws would be fierce and treat my sister cruelly in every way. My sister couldn't bear it any longer and escaped back to her parents' home, vowing never to go back to her in-laws' home. Seeing this situation, we felt sorry for her, so we brought her to Shanghai to make a living. Several years passed, and the other family didn't ask about her. Even when the war broke out in Shanghai, her in-laws turned a deaf ear. Unexpectedly, this spring, the other family contacted me, demanding that my sister be sent back to get married. Sir, my sister now

Page 20

has made up her mind to dissolve the engagement with the other family. However, because the other family has raised my sister for several years, they are demanding compensation for their losses. It seems that if my sister doesn't go home to get married, the other family won't let me go. If I don't acknowledge the compensation for their losses, this matter will become a stalemate, or they might file a lawsuit against me. After much thought, I don't know what to do. Please advise me on a way out. I would be most grateful! Respectfully, Xia Qu.

× × × ×

Editor's Note: Judging from the letter, your sister's fiancé doesn't seem to be stubborn. Although they haven't explicitly agreed to the dissolution of the engagement, the demand for compensation for losses can be seen as an implicit agreement. After the engagement is dissolved, your sister and the other family will naturally have no relationship, so the other family will have no obligation to support her. Their demand for compensation for losses is justified. As for the uncle taking her there without permission, since you didn't immediately object at the time or take effective action, you can't use this as an excuse to shirk responsibility now. At the same time, regarding the abuse, if you have solid evidence to prove that she absolutely couldn't live there, it can naturally be considered the fault of the other family, and you can demand unconditional dissolution of the engagement. Now that many years have passed, the physical evidence is gone, and the testimony of witnesses can't be relied on, so it's really impossible to trace back. Therefore, the best thing to do is to keep the documents they are asking for compensation for losses; the engagement can definitely be dissolved, but the losses must also be compensated. Dissolution of the engagement is one thing, and compensation is another, proceed separately. As for the compensation, there are two points that can be discussed. ⑴ The determination of the amount; the cost of raising her can vary greatly, with anything from ten to over a hundred yuan per year being considered reasonable. It's best to ask an impartial person to act as an intermediary and determine the amount appropriately based on the family's living conditions. ⑵ Discussion of fulfillment; judging from the letter, Mr. Xia doesn't seem to be a wealthy person, so where would he get such a large sum of money at once? You should discuss with the other family to pay in installments. If this matter goes to court in the end, the result will inevitably be "the engagement between the two parties is allowed to be dissolved; the woman should compensate the man for losses of a certain amount (determined by the judge based on the circumstances)." As for the method of payment, it is a matter of enforcement and a matter of fact. If you really can't come up with it, you can't escape the method of paying in installments, and you won't be jailed! But in all honesty, this loss should be compensated; therefore, after the amount is determined, Mr. Xia should try his best to plan. It's not okay to deliberately deceive and try to deny it.

Remnants of Life Under the Pen 192

— Hou Ying

Many people say that frequent dreaming is a sign of mental weakness; however, not dreaming is too depressing. I am a weak person, so I can't help but be overcome by this consolation, however slight! In recent days, I have been dreaming almost every night.

⑴

I stand proudly on the earth, looking out at thousands of mountains and rivers, all faintly hidden in the clouds and mist. All I see before me is red earth for thousands of miles, stretching endlessly. I wander forward, and I look back again; I feel that the vastness of the world is full of crises, conspiracies, and selfishness. Although there is no one here, can you say for sure that there won't be a trap in front of you? The roars of lions and tigers are getting closer and closer.

I don't know when a high mountain appeared before my eyes. The mountain was surrounded by a radiant golden light. My eyes were dazzled, my head was dizzy. Undoubtedly, those who live on top are immortals and gods?

I struggled to support myself and walked forward, but the golden light shrank with my footsteps. Finally, I walked to the bottom of the high mountain, and the golden light disappeared into thin air.

Here, I sit on a stone, looking up. I see capitalists whipping workers, I see thieves robbing in broad daylight: I also see soldiers killing each other; I see people wearing masks, deceiving each other... I feel disappointed in everything. Are humans living in golden light not the same as humans all over the world? My heart is broken! So-called immortals and gods are only like this! I curse the people, and I curse the people on the high mountain even more: I stand up weakly and walk forward blankly. The gentle breeze blows slowly, and the waves in the sea gently ripple. Where will you drift, floating duckweed!

Golden light is born with my feet, and when I look back, it is already shining tens of thousands of feet high. No matter the traitors and thieves, no matter the killings, everything is shrouded in golden light; from the surface, I only feel a purple aura and auspicious clouds. Alas! Hypocrisy! Hypocrisy! I hate you, I curse you! You have killed all of humanity's hearts, you have dirtied the clean land! This world is all your power, where can I find a piece of innocence?

⑵

I am alone, walking among thousands of people. The noisy voices of people hum around me. Several people who look familiar say to me in my ear: "Hou Ying, justice has failed!" I am shocked and turn around to ask: "Really?" But they don't answer and leave by themselves.

I feel annoyed in my heart, like a criminal about to be executed! The rumbling of cannons is endless: smoke rises on all sides, covering the soldiers in battle. They don't know who they are fighting, and I don't know who is fighting whom?

The masses of people are waving flags and shouting in the air; gradually they are divided into two factions. Clearly, the eastern flag bears the words "Power"; while the western flag flutters with "Justice". But alas! There are only two or three hunched-back figures standing under "Justice"!

Needless to say, "Justice" has retreated. During the time when they are insisting without deciding, I see several people jumping out from the "Power" side wearing masks with smiling faces; they stand in the center of the battle, seeming to want to make peace. But I see in their hearts that they are full of wanting to eat these two or three "supporters of justice".

Pain! Serious Injury! National Humiliation, May 5, 5, 5, 30, Xi Yuan! 193

"Justice" failed, they clap their hands and cheer in the air; I can't bear to see it anymore and turn around to leave.

"Power" gradually descends and grabs me up into the clouds. Although I am shocked in my heart, my mind is still clear; therefore, I do not shout or beg for mercy.

In a trance, they throw me down!

Difficult to Submit, Difficult for the Editor 194

— Ping

The other day, Mr. Pengnian's article in this magazine, "The Life of Selling Writing," treated the author as an equal, feeling that selling one's heart's blood is the most miserable profession, and many writers revealed a cry that they dared not raise their voices between the lines. A writer, whether famous or not, squeezes his own brains in the same way when writing articles. The works of famous writers are certainly easier to sell than those of the unknown; the price can also be increased, but there are also difficulties for the famous after they become famous. The crystallization of their brains cannot be scribbled on like the works of the unknown, because their works have been noticed, and they have to grasp people's belief in him. When a work is published, they have to be cautious when starting to write. If they lose their inspection even slightly, they will be scolded by jealous people if their work regresses compared to previous works. The "criticism" in the Chinese literary world is fundamentally transferred by the emotions of the critic and the author: the same faction praises it as a masterpiece of meticulous work, and the opposition scolds it worse than dog excrement. Therefore, a famous writer often publishes a thin book only every year and a half.

As for unknown writers, if you want to squeeze into our literary world, that is difficult, difficult, and the third one is still difficult. They all take the supplements of various newspapers as experimental grounds. Although it is relatively easy to publish, they must first understand the purpose of various supplements when writing, and should cater to their preferences and not go against them. After the manuscript is sent out, they look forward to seeing their name on the list of successes every day. The taste of that disappointment and expectation is only understood by those who have experienced it, and I apologize for not being able to describe this state of mind that is both surprised and happy. Imagine that you are full of good works that you think will make you stand out, but are closed in the wastebasket by the editor, and you will naturally be angry. If you encounter obstacles again and again, you will get angry at the editor for not having eyes, worshiping idols, and taking care of friends. This is the editor's undeserved disaster. Many people say: "To be an editor, you only need to have the power to appreciate words!" I am not afraid of being thick-skinned, and I have also been a supplement editor for three months. In addition to the power to appreciate words, you must have the ability to "see everywhere and listen to all directions." You must also be able to accept scolding and endure anger, otherwise, please step down. Although I cannot represent all the editors in admitting that editors worship idols, it is inevitable to some extent. (May I ask Buddha-kun if he thinks so?) There is probably no reason why the manuscripts of friends are not taken care of a little, and it is not that the editors are not afraid of being scolded. This is exactly where it is difficult to be an editor! The selection of manuscripts must keep up with the times, catch the tide, and cater to the readers, but sometimes "I want both fish and bear's paw", and the space is limited, so the act of cutting it out with a heavy heart and causing injustice to sink to the bottom is common, and those who scold you will definitely not let you go. It is not easy to submit, and it is also difficult to edit!

Shop Clerk Communications

Prison Visit 195

Editor: My friend, Mr. Someone, was detained for gambling and sentenced to five months in prison. Yesterday, his wife went to visit him and learned that he was seriously ill in prison. He lacks both caretakers and medicine, and his life and future are worrying. I have come to consult with you, intending to visit him together and seek a remedy. However, because of the regulation that "family visits are limited to once a month at most", we were turned away. I think that Mr. Someone's crime is not punishable by death, and I cannot bear to let him die of illness in prison. I wonder if there is any remedy? Please advise! (Sincerely, Hu Zhengzhi)

× × ×

Editor's Note: In ancient times, criminal policy adopted a retributive approach; in the Middle Ages, it adopted a suppressive approach, sparing no harsh punishments, believing it was a plan to punish one as a warning to a hundred. In modern times, humanitarianism is gradually becoming more popular, and criminal policy is also adopting a reformative approach. Except for a few criminals who "are unlikely to repent" and are sentenced to death, the rest are sentenced to varying terms of imprisonment. During the execution period, reformative education is applied, and the highest principle is to "make the prisoner a pillar of society after being released from prison". Therefore, both the physical and mental health of the prisoner must be taken into account. Although prisons in various places have various regulations for the sake of easy management, they must not violate this principle in the end. The prison that Mr. Hu mentioned may have a regulation that "family visits are limited to once a month at most"; but there must be other regulations for sick prisoners to provide relief. However, unscrupulous prison officials saw that you did not understand the regulations and deliberately made things difficult, wanting to make some money. The best thing to do now is to submit a petition to the court, apply for release for medical treatment; and also hire a lawyer - not necessarily a very famous one, it will cost too much money! Accompany them on the visit. With someone who is familiar with the law as a companion, the prison officials will not dare to cheat.
