Movie Special

Little Van朋克 Accused of Seducing Another Man's Wife After Losing His Own 196

Little Van朋克's luck has been truly bad recently. After announcing his separation from Joan Crawford, he is now being sued by a German singer named Jorgen Dietz, who accuses him of seducing his ex-wife, leading to their divorce, and demands compensation of 60,000 yuan. However, Little Van朋克's attitude is also very stubborn. He says this is pure extortion, and that movie stars have always been blackmailed, even when innocent, they would rather pay some money to settle privately for the sake of peace. But he wants to be motivated from now on to break this bad habit. Of course, many people in Hollywood hope that Little Van朋克 can win, because he has a lot of evidence that can prove that both parties are suspected of extortion.

Little Van朋克 said, "I know Alma Telma, Jorgen Dietz's ex-wife. We met in a film studio, just like I met countless other men and women. But to say that I would pick her out of thousands of women to be my sweetheart or future wife is out of the question. I can't just meet a woman, say a few words to her, and have it count as if I've already agreed to marry her."

When Jorgen Dietz first said that Little Van朋克 had seduced his wife and wanted him to pay for a settlement, Jorgen went to see Van's manager. He said that Van must pay up, because Van caused him to lose his wife and must remarry, but he had no money for the wedding. Van's manager, hearing Jorgen Dietz's words, knew that his purpose was to extort money, so he decided not to give money and would rather go to court. However, that manager, for the sake of prudence, consulted with a local prosecutor, who sent someone to investigate the matter. Later, Jorgen Dietz brought a woman named 露惜都蘭, who married Jorgen Dietz after Jorgen Dietz and Alma Telma divorced. This new couple came to Little Van朋克's place and insisted on selling jewelry worth 300 yuan to Little Van朋克 for 6,000 yuan. At that time, the representative of the local prosecutor was present and witnessed the matter. As a result, Little Van朋克 and his manager were willing to pay 1,500 yuan to buy it. Jorgen Dietz agreed and immediately paid a check, and both parties concluded the case. However, after Jorgen Dietz and his wife left, they were taken away for questioning by the representative of the local prosecutor. Therefore, Jorgen Dietz sued Little Van朋克, demanding compensation for the loss of his wife of 5,000 yuan. Another 1,000 yuan for illegal detention, totaling 6,000 yuan.

Little Van朋克 said, "If I am guilty, I would of course be willing to pay a few thousand dollars to settle the case. But this matter is entirely extortion. How can I give in? You must know that the time and lawyer fees I have spent on this case are definitely more than just a few thousand dollars."

Review of "Explosion Machine" 197

— 思蘋

The plot, direction, acting, and photography are all excellent

The Nanjing Grand Theater premiered Fox Company's "Explosion Machine" yesterday. It is a good film that satirizes life in the style of Bernard Shaw. The film's plot is humorous, the direction is perfect, the acting is natural, and the photography's technique and light are soft and reach the top level. The title "Explosion Machine" seems to suggest a "thrilling" supernatural film, but in reality, it is not.

The screenplay of this film is divided into two segments. The first, shorter section can be said to be the prologue, narrating how an American teenager, Robert, travels in Paris and encounters a beautiful woman, Eleanor, due to a car accident. This American teenager secretly boards a mail ship in pursuit of love, and thus the film introduces the larger, later segment, which is the main plot of "Explosion Machine." The main plot of "Explosion Machine" takes a large ship braving the waves as its backdrop, and the various passengers on the ship as its characters. The unpredictable nature of life can thus be naturally depicted. Its subject matter is similar to "Grand Hotel."

The subject matter of "Explosion Machine" mainly utilizes humanity's weakness of fearing death and clinging to life. The ship's radio operator fabricates a telegram saying that someone is plotting to blow up the ship in the middle of the night, implying the end of the world in people's minds. Thus, the captain with a chronic illness who is about to die, the veterinary professor, the wealthy man who exploits the poor, the old aunt who is afraid of death, the singer with a crisp voice! Each passenger suspects each other, each expressing the fear of an impending doomsday hidden in their minds, as well as the various ugly behaviors that humans should reveal at the critical moment of life and death. Humanity's selfish and self-interested base nature is thus displayed without reservation.

Roses have thorns, and the path of love is full of thorns. Robert and Eleanor's love in the film "Explosion Machine" is also depicted tortuously and naturally according to this idea. Many movie stars, such as John Barrymore, only know how to act with a straight face, and many movie stars, such as 雷門那伐樂, always like to perform with a smiling face. In this film, the young actor 吉士德馬烈斯 plays the American teenager with a sense of humor, maintaining his original acting style. The other actors, such as 琴娜 陶屏 who plays Eleanor, are able to express the different characteristics of the characters in the play. In the dialogue, several silent fragments are inserted to narrate the backgrounds of the characters in the play, which is more convenient than introducing them scene by scene. As for the dialogue in the film, it is indeed very witty, but it feels a bit too much. The most dramatic point of this film lies in the suspended theme of the end of the world, in grasping a kind of suspicion on the ship, and depicting it scene by scene, culminating in the discovery that it is just a castle in the air, a false alarm.

Review of "Lipstick Market" 198

—凌鶴

A better work among sound films

The director has made significant progress

After Star Film Company raised the issue of women's liberation in "A Woman's Cry," it has re-raised this issue in "Lipstick Market." We will not forget that in "A Woman's Cry" we heard the painful wails of petty-bourgeois women, but there was no "cry" at all. So, how is this issue resolved in "Lipstick Market" when it is raised again? The development of the plot clearly tells us that when Li Cuifen's family finances are completely bankrupt, she runs out of her beautiful student life and becomes a saleswoman in a department store. She is insulted, ridiculed, or satirized by people, so in order to maintain her identity as a "pure and innocent girl," she is determined not to do it. However, the whip of life constantly whips her, and at the same time, inspired by Miss Yang, she still has to continue to struggle, so she picks tea, copies, and answers the phone, and she hopes to move towards a bright future in her own hard work. If the plot ends here, undoubtedly it has grasped reality and explained that so-called "equality between men and women" is just a lie in real society. That is, there is no way to solve the problem of women's liberation in real society. However, this play does not end like this. It actually enables Li Cuifen to save money in the bank from her extremely meager personal income, in addition to dealing with the daily expenses of a family of three, and finally even opens a foreign goods store, and the mother and daughter enjoy peace and prosperity.

Obviously, this is a work that praises real society, completely obliterating the current most serious economic panic, especially whitewashing the reality that the current national economy is almost completely bankrupt. Honestly, no one can believe that a female worker can actually save up. Using golden dreams to explain the future of working women, I think Mr. Ding Qianping, the screenwriter of "Torrent," would not dream like this.

Director Zhang Shichuan's progress can be seen in this film to some extent, at least more technically advanced than "Lovesickness". However, because he pays too much attention to the actors' expressions, I always feel that the dialogue and performance are not very connected. However, the shots are very good, especially a few close-ups.

The scenery in the clerk's residence is a failure, it should never be so gorgeous. The sound is still good. Some of the dialogues are very forced, and they are still the same sudden empty shouts of "darkness" and "light". The subtitles are very appropriate. The photography is also very good. Most of the actors are generally okay, but they are always too relaxed. On the whole, the technique is better among Chinese sound films, and it will not be too disappointing.

Naoma Shearer Talks About Dreams 199

—康冰

"When I was in high school in Canada, many classmates planned to go boating on the weekend," Naoma Shearer said. "But the night before, I had a strange dream. I sank in the river, and my mother wanted to save me, but she also fell into the water. Fortunately, a stranger came and rescued us. This person had a very deep scar on the left side of his face. I woke up like this."

"The dream was very clear. I didn't close my eyes that night. The next morning, I felt it was not a good sign. My mother thought it was best to stay at home and not go boating."

"That afternoon they went boating, but I didn't go. Later, the wind and waves were very strong, and the boat hit a reef. Many friends fell into the river and became ill as a result. One of my closest girlfriends was very ill. Strangely enough, she also had the same nightmare as me on Thursday night, but she didn't care. What surprised me even more was that when the boat owner came to visit her, his face was exactly the same as the person I saw in my dream, with a very deep scar on the left side of his face."

Submission Guidelines for the Shen Bao Movie Supplement 200

This supplement is a movie publication that assists in cultural promotion and artistic expression. External manuscripts are very welcome. Once published, generous remuneration will be provided. Once a text is published, the copyright belongs to Shen Bao. The language of the text should be vernacular Chinese and must use modern punctuation. If the submitted article is a translation, the original should be attached, and English should be omitted if possible. Due to the limited space of this supplement, the text should be as concise as possible, with each manuscript limited to approximately 500 characters. Unless otherwise stated in advance and postage for a reply is attached, text, photos, etc. will not be returned. If plagiarism or verbatim transcription is discovered, no remuneration will be provided. When submitting a manuscript, each article must be stamped, otherwise it will not be remunerated. Do not write on both sides of the paper or write horizontally.

The Secrets of Movie Novels (Secrets) (9) 201

— Cairo

"If that's the case, please rest assured. I will absolutely not obstruct my husband's will."

"That's very good, thank you." Martina was extremely happy. She seemed to have won a great victory, and walked out cheerfully. But before she could leave, John had already run in, panting. He came in and shouted "Mary" first! But Martina put on a very flattering pose, telling him that Mary had agreed to let him be free. John asked, "Free, let me be free?" He stared at Mary.

Martina said: "Yes, my love, you are free, you can marry me, isn't that good!" "Mary"! John shouted in a lost voice. But Mary stood still, silently looking at him. John turned back and grabbed Martina's arm, rebuking angrily: "What did you tell her? What nonsense are you talking? Tell me!"

"John, don't do this"! Mary softly advised her husband. John heard it. He immediately released Martina's arm and took a step back. Martina then said? "I told her you love me, you are willing to marry me, you want to be free, is all this nonsense?" Martina's eyes showed some arrogance. "It's all nonsense! These words, and many other words, are all lies I said"! The woman's attitude immediately changed, glaring at John angrily and said: "Okay, in front of your own wife, you are like this"! "Even if you call me to kneel before God, I will say the same thing. What I said to you was all nonsense when I was confused. We are breaking off relations from now on, it is over, it is gone."

Martina heard it, as if a bucket of cold water had been poured on her back. She said angrily: "This is a righteous gentleman, and he still wants to be the governor of a province! Hmph, I can explain this matter. Do you know, it is not difficult for me to ruin your reputation." After she finished speaking, her eyes were full of murderous light, staring at John. "I know," Mary said calmly. "He knows it well." "Putting this story in the newspaper would be good news. I will make you unable to become governor!" Martina said, and turned back to Mary, "Mrs. Carton, you can keep your husband as much as you want, as long as you are willing to have him." "That's very good, thank you." Mary replied in Martina's tone a few minutes ago, in which there was endless meaning, causing different feelings in the hearts of the two women. Martina retreated. John opened the door, his face full of shame towards his beloved wife, but Mary did not blame him. She said that she had known about this matter a long time ago. She also knew her husband. Even when he was thousands of miles away, and was confused by the beauty of women, he had never forgotten his beloved wife at home for a moment. Saying this made John extremely grateful to her.
